# Clean package cache and install required packages
dnf clean all
dnf install -y python3 python3-pip python3-libselinux sudo curl wget tar unzip vim

# Set Python 3 as default python
alternatives --set python /usr/bin/python3 2>/dev/null || ln -sf /usr/bin/python3 /usr/bin/python

# Verify Python installation
python3 --version && python --version

# Expected output:
# Python 3.6.x (Oracle Linux 8)
# or
# Python 3.9.x (Oracle Linux 9)


# Fix hostname resolution (ensure hostname resolves correctly)

# On oracle8 (192.168.121.150):
hostnamectl set-hostname oracle8.local

cat > /etc/hosts << 'EOF'
127.0.0.1   localhost localhost.localdomain
127.0.1.1   oracle8.local oracle8
::1         localhost localhost.localdomain
EOF


# On oracle9 (192.168.121.177):
hostnamectl set-hostname oracle9.local

cat > /etc/hosts << 'EOF'
127.0.0.1   localhost localhost.localdomain
127.0.1.1   oracle9.local oracle9
::1         localhost localhost.localdomain
EOF


# Test svc_ans account
su - svc_ans -c "sudo whoami"

# Expected output:
# root


VERIFICATION:
-------------

# Verify svc_ans user:
id svc_ans

# Verify wheel group membership:
groups svc_ans
# Expected: svc_ans : svc_ans wheel

# Verify passwordless sudo:
su - svc_ans -c "sudo whoami"
# Expected: root (no password prompt)

# Verify Python:
python3 --version
python --version


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 5.4: SSH KEY GENERATION AND DISTRIBUTION
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Generate SSH key pair on control node and distribute to all managed nodes

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node

SECURITY: 4096-bit RSA key for strong security


# Switch to svc_ans user on control node
su - svc_ans

# Verify current user
whoami
# Expected: svc_ans


# Generate SSH key pair (4096-bit RSA, no passphrase)
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096 -f ~/.ssh/id_rsa -N "" -C "ansible-svc_ans-key"

# Expected output:
# Generating public/private rsa key pair.
# Your identification has been saved in /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
# Your public key has been saved in /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
# The key fingerprint is:
# SHA256:<fingerprint> ansible-svc_ans-key
# The key's randomart image is:
# +---[RSA 4096]----+
# | ...             |
# | ...             |
# +----[SHA256]-----+


# Verify key files created
ls -la ~/.ssh/

# Expected output:
# total 16
# drwx------ 2 svc_ans svc_ans 4096 <date> .
# drwx------ 3 svc_ans svc_ans 4096 <date> ..
# -rw------- 1 svc_ans svc_ans 3243 <date> id_rsa      # Private key
# -rw-r--r-- 1 svc_ans svc_ans  749 <date> id_rsa.pub  # Public key


# Distribute public key to all managed nodes
# You will be prompted for svc_ans password on each host

ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@192.168.68.110

# Expected output:
# /usr/bin/ssh-copy-id: INFO: Source of key(s) to be installed: "/home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa.pub"
# /usr/bin/ssh-copy-id: INFO: attempting to log in with the new key(s), to filter out any that are already installed
# /usr/bin/ssh-copy-id: INFO: 1 key(s) remain to be installed -- if you are prompted now it is to install the new keys
# svc_ans@192.168.68.110's password: [enter password]
# Number of key(s) added: 1
# Now try logging into the machine, with: "ssh 'svc_ans@192.168.68.110'"


ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@192.168.121.164
# Enter password when prompted

ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@192.168.121.150
# Enter password when prompted

ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@192.168.121.177
# Enter password when prompted

# Loop alternative:

for host in 192.168.68.110 192.168.121.164 192.168.121.150 192.168.121.177; do
      echo ">>> Copying SSH key to $host"
      ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@$host
  done


# Populate known_hosts file (prevents "unknown host" prompts)
for host in 192.168.68.110 192.168.121.164 192.168.121.150 192.168.121.177; do
    ssh-keyscan -H "$host" >> ~/.ssh/known_hosts
done

# Expected output:
# # 192.168.68.110:22 SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_x.x
# # 192.168.68.110:22 SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_x.x
# # 192.168.68.110:22 SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_x.x
# ... (3 lines per host - different key types)


# Verify known_hosts file
cat ~/.ssh/known_hosts | wc -l

# Expected: >= 12 lines (3 per host × 4 hosts)


# Test passwordless SSH to all hosts
for host in 192.168.68.110 192.168.121.164 192.168.121.150 192.168.121.177; do
    echo "=== Testing $host ==="
    ssh $host "hostname && whoami && sudo whoami"
done

# Expected output for each host:
# === Testing 192.168.68.110 ===
# ubuntu22       (hostname)
# svc_ans        (current user)
# root           (sudo whoami)
#
# === Testing 192.168.121.164 ===
# ubuntu24
# svc_ans
# root
#
# === Testing 192.168.121.150 ===
# oracle8
# svc_ans
# root
#
# === Testing 192.168.121.177 ===
# oracle9
# svc_ans
# root

# If any host prompts for password, SSH key distribution failed for that host
# Re-run ssh-copy-id for that host


# Create SSH client configuration for optimized connections
cat > ~/.ssh/config << 'EOF'
Host *
    IdentityFile          /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
    StrictHostKeyChecking no
    UserKnownHostsFile    /home/svc_ans/.ssh/known_hosts
    ServerAliveInterval   60
    ServerAliveCountMax   3
    ConnectTimeout        10
EOF

# Set permissions on config file
chmod 600 ~/.ssh/config

# Verify config file
cat ~/.ssh/config


# Exit from svc_ans user back to root
exit


SSH CONFIG EXPLAINED:
---------------------

IdentityFile          : Use this private key for all connections
StrictHostKeyChecking : Don't prompt for unknown hosts (already in known_hosts)
UserKnownHostsFile    : Use this known_hosts file
ServerAliveInterval   : Send keepalive every 60 seconds
ServerAliveCountMax   : Disconnect after 3 missed keepalives
ConnectTimeout        : Timeout connection after 10 seconds


VERIFICATION:
-------------

# As svc_ans user on control node:
su - svc_ans

# Test passwordless SSH (should not prompt for anything):
ssh 192.168.68.110 echo "SSH to ubuntu22 works"
ssh 192.168.121.164 echo "SSH to ubuntu24 works"
ssh 192.168.121.150 echo "SSH to oracle8 works"
ssh 192.168.121.177 echo "SSH to oracle9 works"

# Test sudo on remote hosts:
ssh 192.168.68.110 "sudo whoami"
# Expected: root

exit


TROUBLESHOOTING:
----------------

# If SSH prompts for password:

# 1. Verify public key was copied to remote host:
ssh svc_ans@<host> "cat ~/.ssh/authorized_keys"
# Should show your public key

# 2. Check permissions on remote host:
ssh svc_ans@<host> "ls -la ~/.ssh/"
# .ssh should be 700
# authorized_keys should be 600

# 3. Re-copy key:
ssh-copy-id -i ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub svc_ans@<host>


# If "Host key verification failed":

# Remove host from known_hosts:
ssh-keygen -R <host>

# Re-add host:
ssh-keyscan -H <host> >> ~/.ssh/known_hosts

SECTION 5.5: JENKINS SSH SETUP
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Configure Jenkins user to access managed nodes via SSH

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node as root

NOTE: Jenkins will use svc_ans SSH key for Ansible operations


# Create .ssh directory for Jenkins user
mkdir -p /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh
chown jenkins:jenkins /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh
chmod 700 /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh

# Verify permissions
ls -ld /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh

# Expected output:
# drwx------ 2 jenkins jenkins 4096 <date> /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh


# Create known_hosts file for Jenkins
touch /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts
chown jenkins:jenkins /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts
chmod 644 /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts


# Populate Jenkins known_hosts with all managed node keys
for host in 192.168.68.110 192.168.121.164 192.168.121.150 192.168.121.177; do
    ssh-keyscan "$host" >> /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts
done

# Expected output:
# # 192.168.68.110:22 SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_x.x
# # 192.168.68.110:22 SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_x.x
# ... (3 lines per host)


# Verify known_hosts file
sudo -u jenkins wc -l /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts

# Expected: >= 12 lines (3 key types × 4 hosts)


# Verify Jenkins user can read known_hosts
sudo -u jenkins cat /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts | head -5


VERIFICATION:
-------------

# Verify Jenkins SSH directory structure:
ls -la /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/

# Expected output:
# total 12
# drwx------ 2 jenkins jenkins 4096 <date> .
# drwxr-x--- 3 jenkins jenkins 4096 <date> ..
# -rw-r--r-- 1 jenkins jenkins 1234 <date> known_hosts


# Verify Jenkins can read svc_ans inventory files (will be created in Part 6):
# This will be tested after Ansible setup


SERVICE ACCOUNT SETUP COMPLETE:

================================================================================
PART 6: DUAL ANSIBLE INSTALLATION (2.9 + 6.7)
================================================================================

This section installs two versions of Ansible side-by-side:
- Ansible 2.9.27 (system installation via yum) - for Ubuntu 22, Oracle 8/9
- Ansible 6.7.0 (virtual environment via pip) - for Ubuntu 24

ARCHITECTURE:
- System Ansible (2.9): /usr/bin/ansible
- Venv Ansible (6.7): /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible

BENEFITS:
- Backward compatibility (existing 2.9 playbooks work)
- Ubuntu 24 support (requires Ansible 6.7)
- No conflicts between versions
- Easy version selection in Jenkins pipeline

PREREQUISITES:
- Service account (svc_ans) configured (Part 5 completed)
- Python 3 available on control node


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 6.1: ANSIBLE 2.9.27 (SYSTEM INSTALLATION)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Install Ansible 2.9 from system repository for Ubuntu 22, Oracle 8/9

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node as root

# Complete!

----------------

SECTION 6.3: CREATE ANSIBLE 6.7 VIRTUAL ENVIRONMENT
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create isolated Python virtual environment for Ansible 6.7

EXECUTION: Run commands as root initially, then as svc_ans

python3.11 -m venv /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv

# Expected output:
# (no output means success)


# Verify virtual environment created
ls -la /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv

# Expected output:

# drwxr-xr-x  3 root    root    4096 <date> lib
# drwxr-xr-x  3 root    root    4096 <date> lib64

# Set ownership to svc_ans
chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv

ls -ld /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv

whoami

# Expected output:

which python

# Expected output:

# Expected output:

# Expected output:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 6.4: ANSIBLE CONFIGURATION FILES
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create Ansible configuration files for both versions

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node


CONFIGURATION STRATEGY:
- Ansible 2.9: Uses /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg
- Ansible 6.7: Uses /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg
- Separate configs allow version-specific settings


As svc_ans (for Ansible 6.7 in venv):
--------------------------------------

# Switch to svc_ans
su - svc_ans

# Virtual environment should auto-activate (due to .bashrc)
# Prompt: (ansible-venv) [svc_ans@jenkinspreprod ~]$


# Create Ansible configuration for venv Ansible 6.7

cat > ~/ansible.cfg << 'EOF'
# ==============================================================================
# ANSIBLE CONFIGURATION - ANSIBLE 6.7.0 (Virtual Environment)
# Purpose: Ubuntu 24 Support + Modern Ansible Features
# Virtual Environment: /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv
# ==============================================================================
[defaults]
inventory             = /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts
remote_user           = svc_ans
host_key_checking     = False
private_key_file      = /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
interpreter_python    = auto_silent
stdout_callback       = ansible.builtin.default
result_format         = yaml
bin_ansible_callbacks = True
log_path              = /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log
collections_paths     = /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/collections:/home/svc_ans/.ansible/collections

[inventory]
enable_plugins = host_list, script, auto, yaml, ini

[privilege_escalation]
become          = True
become_method   = sudo
become_user     = root
become_ask_pass = False

[ssh_connection]
pipelining   = True
control_path = %(directory)s/%%h-%%p-%%r
EOF
==================================================================

Not working

cat > ~/ansible.cfg << 'EOF'

# ANSIBLE CONFIGURATION - ANSIBLE 6.7.0 (Virtual Environment)

# ==============================================================================

[defaults]

host_key_checking     = False
private_key_file      = /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
interpreter_python    = auto_silent
stdout_callback       = yaml
bin_ansible_callbacks = True
log_path              = /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log

# Collections path - use venv collections
collections_paths     = /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/collections:/home/svc_ans/.ansible/collections

[inventory]
enable_plugins = host_list, script, auto, yaml, ini

[privilege_escalation]
become          = True
become_method   = sudo
become_user     = root
become_ask_pass = False

[ssh_connection]

As root (for Ansible 2.9 system):
----------------------------------

# Create Ansible configuration for system Ansible 2.9
cat > /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg << 'EOF'
# ==============================================================================
# ANSIBLE CONFIGURATION - ANSIBLE 2.9.27 (System Installation)
# Purpose: Ubuntu 22, Oracle Linux 8/9 Support
# ==============================================================================

[defaults]
inventory          = /etc/ansible/hosts
remote_user        = svc_ans
private_key_file   = /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
host_key_checking  = False
interpreter_python = auto_silent
log_path           = /var/log/ansible.log

[privilege_escalation]
become          = True
become_method   = sudo
become_user     = root
become_ask_pass = False

[ssh_connection]
pipelining   = True
control_path = /tmp/ansible-ssh-%h-%p-%r
EOF


# Verify configuration file created
cat /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg


CONFIGURATION PARAMETERS EXPLAINED:
------------------------------------

inventory:
  - Path to Ansible inventory file
  - Different for each version (separation of concerns)

remote_user:
  - User account for SSH connections
  - svc_ans for both versions

host_key_checking:
  - Disable strict host key checking
  - Allows connections to new hosts without prompts

private_key_file:
  - SSH private key for authentication
  - Same key used by both versions

interpreter_python:
  - auto_silent: Automatically detect Python interpreter on target
  - Prevents warnings about Python discovery

stdout_callback:
  - yaml: Format output as YAML (easier to read)

collections_paths (6.7 only):
  - Search venv collections first, then user collections

become:
  - Enable privilege escalation (sudo)
  - Required for most system administration tasks

pipelining:
  - Reduce number of SSH connections
  - Improves performance significantly


VERIFICATION:
-------------

# As root, verify system Ansible uses system config:
ansible --version | grep "config file"

# Expected output:
# config file = /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg


# As svc_ans, verify venv Ansible uses venv config:
su - svc_ans
ansible --version | grep "config file"

# Expected output:
# config file = /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg

exit

SECTION 6.5: ANSIBLE INVENTORY
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create Ansible inventory with all managed nodes

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node as root


# Create Ansible directory for svc_ans
mkdir -p /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks
mkdir -p /home/svc_ans/logs


# Create comprehensive Ansible inventory
cat > /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts << 'EOF'
# ==============================================================================
# ANSIBLE INVENTORY - MULTI-OS ENVIRONMENT
# Control Node: jenkinspreprod.local (Oracle Linux 8.10)
# Managed Nodes: Ubuntu 22/24, Oracle Linux 8/9
# ==============================================================================

# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# UBUNTU 22.04 LTS SERVERS (Ansible 2.9)
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[ubuntu22]
192.168.68.110 ansible_host=192.168.68.110

[ubuntu22:vars]
ansible_python_interpreter=/usr/bin/python3


# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# UBUNTU 24.04 LTS SERVERS (Ansible 6.7 - Virtual Environment)
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[ubuntu24]
192.168.121.164 ansible_host=192.168.121.164

[ubuntu24:vars]
ansible_python_interpreter=/usr/bin/python3
use_ansible_venv=true


# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# ORACLE LINUX 8 SERVERS (Ansible 2.9)
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[oracle8]
192.168.121.150 ansible_host=192.168.121.150

[oracle8:vars]
ansible_python_interpreter=/usr/bin/python3.6


# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# ORACLE LINUX 9 SERVERS (Ansible 2.9)
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[oracle9]
192.168.121.177 ansible_host=192.168.121.177

[oracle9:vars]
ansible_python_interpreter=/usr/bin/python3.9


# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# LOGICAL GROUPINGS
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[ubuntu:children]
ubuntu22
ubuntu24

[oracle:children]
oracle8
oracle9

[all_linux:children]
ubuntu
oracle


# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# GLOBAL VARIABLES (APPLY TO ALL HOSTS)
# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
[all:vars]
ansible_user=svc_ans
ansible_become=yes
ansible_become_method=sudo
ansible_ssh_private_key_file=/home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
EOF


# Copy inventory to /etc/ansible for system Ansible
cp /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts /etc/ansible/hosts


# Set ownership and permissions
chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/ansible
chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/logs

chmod 755 /home/svc_ans
chmod 755 /home/svc_ans/ansible
chmod 755 /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks
chmod 644 /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts


# Verify Jenkins user can read inventory
sudo -u jenkins cat /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts | head -10


INVENTORY STRUCTURE EXPLAINED:
-------------------------------

HOST GROUPS:
- [ubuntu22]: Ubuntu 22 hosts (use Ansible 2.9)
- [ubuntu24]: Ubuntu 24 hosts (use Ansible 6.7 venv)
- [oracle8]: Oracle Linux 8 hosts (use Ansible 2.9)
- [oracle9]: Oracle Linux 9 hosts (use Ansible 2.9)

LOGICAL GROUPS:
- [ubuntu:children]: All Ubuntu hosts (22 + 24)
- [oracle:children]: All Oracle Linux hosts (8 + 9)
- [all_linux:children]: All Linux hosts

GROUP VARIABLES:
- ansible_python_interpreter: Python path on target
- use_ansible_venv: Flag for wrapper script (ubuntu24)

GLOBAL VARIABLES [all:vars]:
- ansible_user: SSH user (svc_ans)
- ansible_become: Enable sudo
- ansible_become_method: Use sudo for privilege escalation
- ansible_ssh_private_key_file: SSH key path

TROUBLESHOOTING:
----------------

# If ping fails:

# 1. Verify SSH connectivity:
su - svc_ans
ssh 192.168.68.110 echo "test"

# 2. Verify inventory syntax:
ansible all --list-hosts -i ~/ansible/hosts

# 3. Verify Python on target:
ssh 192.168.68.110 "which python3 && python3 --version"

# 4. Run with verbose output:
ansible all -m ping -vvv


# If "Permission denied":

# 1. Verify SSH key permissions:
ls -la ~/.ssh/id_rsa
# Should be: -rw------- (600)

# 2. Verify SSH key is in authorized_keys on target:
ssh 192.168.68.110 "cat ~/.ssh/authorized_keys"


# If "UNREACHABLE":

# 1. Verify firewall allows SSH:
# On Ubuntu: iptables -L -n | grep 22
# On Oracle: firewall-cmd --list-services | grep ssh

# 2. Verify target host is accessible:
ping -c 2 192.168.68.110

# As svc_ans on control node

# Test batch connectivity
for host in 192.168.68.110 192.168.121.164 192.168.121.150 192.168.121.177; do
    echo "====== Testing $host ======"
    ssh -o BatchMode=yes -o ConnectTimeout=5 $host "
        echo 'Hostname: \$(hostname)'
        echo 'User: \$(whoami)'
        echo 'Sudo: \$(sudo whoami)'
        echo 'Python: \$(python3 --version)'
        echo 'Uptime: \$(uptime | cut -d',' -f1)'
    " || echo "FAILED to connect to $host"
    echo ""
done

TROUBLESHOOTING COMMON ISSUES:
-------------------------------

Issue: "Permission denied (publickey)"
Solution: Re-run ssh-copy-id for that host

Issue: "sudo: a password is required"
Solution: Verify /etc/sudoers.d/svc_ans exists and has NOPASSWD:ALL

Issue: "Connection timed out"
Solution: Verify firewall allows SSH from control node

Issue: "python3: command not found"
Solution: Install Python 3 on target node

SECTION 8.1: GROUP VARIABLES

# Create group_vars directory

Ubuntu 22 Variables:
--------------------

cat > /home/svc_ans/ansible/group_vars/ubuntu22.yml << 'EOF'
---
# ==============================================================================
# GROUP VARIABLES - UBUNTU 22.04 LTS
# ==============================================================================

# OS Information
os_family: "ubuntu"
os_version: "22.04"
package_manager: "apt"
ansible_version_required: "2.9"

# Python Interpreter
ansible_python_interpreter: /usr/bin/python3

# Patching Configuration
security_updates_only: false
reboot_after_patch: true
reboot_timeout: 600

# SSH Configuration
ansible_ssh_common_args: '-o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o UserKnownHostsFile=/dev/null'
EOF

# Verify file created
cat /home/svc_ans/ansible/group_vars/ubuntu22.yml

--------------------

# OS Information

os_version: "24.04"
package_manager: "apt"
ansible_version_required: "6.7"

# Python Interpreter (CRITICAL for Ubuntu 24)

# Patching Configuration
security_updates_only: false
reboot_after_patch: true
reboot_timeout: 600

# SSH Configuration

EOF

GROUP VARIABLES EXPLAINED:
---------------------------

os_family:
  - Identifies OS type
  - Used in playbook conditionals

os_version:
  - Specific OS version
  - For version-specific tasks

package_manager:
  - Package manager to use (apt/dnf)
  - For OS-specific package installation

ansible_version_required:
  - Minimum Ansible version needed
  - Documents version compatibility

ansible_python_interpreter:
  - Python path on target host
  - CRITICAL: Prevents interpreter discovery warnings
  - Different for each OS type

security_updates_only:
  - If true, only install security updates
  - Currently set to false (all updates)

reboot_after_patch:
  - Automatically reboot if updates require it
  - Set to true for automated patching

reboot_timeout:
  - How long to wait for reboot (seconds)
  - 600 seconds = 10 minutes

use_ansible_venv (ubuntu24 only):
  - Flag for Jenkins/wrapper to use venv Ansible
  - Only needed for Ubuntu 24


VERIFICATION:
-------------

# Test variable inheritance
su - svc_ans

# Check Ubuntu 22 variables
ansible ubuntu22 -i ~/ansible/hosts -m debug -a "var=os_family"

# Expected output:
# 192.168.68.110 | SUCCESS => {
#     "os_family": "ubuntu"
# }


# Check Ubuntu 24 variables
ansible ubuntu24 -i ~/ansible/hosts -m debug -a "var=ansible_version_required"

# Expected output:
# 192.168.121.164 | SUCCESS => {
#     "ansible_version_required": "6.7"
# }


# Check Oracle 8 variables
ansible oracle8 -i ~/ansible/hosts -m debug -a "var=ansible_python_interpreter"

# Expected output:
# 192.168.121.150 | SUCCESS => {
#     "ansible_python_interpreter": "/usr/bin/python3.6"
# }


exit


INVENTORY AND GROUP_VARS STRUCTURE:
------------------------------------

/home/svc_ans/ansible/
├── hosts                 # Inventory file
├── group_vars/
│   ├── ubuntu22.yml      # Ubuntu 22 specific variables
│   ├── ubuntu24.yml      # Ubuntu 24 specific variables
│   ├── oracle8.yml       # Oracle 8 specific variables
│   └── oracle9.yml       # Oracle 9 specific variables
├── playbooks/            # Playbooks directory (next section)
└── logs/                 # Ansible logs

/etc/ansible/
├── ansible.cfg           # System Ansible 2.9 config
└── hosts                 # Copy of inventory

2. Host variables (if any) override group variables

================================================================================
PART 9: PRODUCTION PLAYBOOKS (LEGACY + MODERN)
================================================================================

This section creates production-grade Ansible playbooks that work with both
Ansible 2.9 (legacy) and Ansible 6.7 (modern), supporting unified OS patching
across Ubuntu 22/24 and Oracle Linux 8/9.

PLAYBOOK STRATEGY:
- Single unified playbook compatible with both Ansible versions
- OS-specific tasks using conditionals (ansible_os_family)
- Reboot handling for both Debian and RedHat families
- Comprehensive logging and verification
- Production-grade error handling

PREREQUISITES:
- Ansible installed (both versions) - Part 6 completed
- Inventory and group_vars configured - Parts 6 and 8 completed
- Managed nodes prepared - Part 7 completed


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 9.1: UNIFIED OS PATCHING PLAYBOOK (PRODUCTION GRADE)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create comprehensive OS patching playbook compatible with both Ansible versions

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node as root


# Create playbooks directory
mkdir -p /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks
mkdir -p /etc/ansible/playbooks


# Create unified production playbook
cat > /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml << 'EOF'
---
################################################################################
# PLAYBOOK: Unified OS Patching for Ubuntu 22/24 and Oracle Linux 8/9
# Description: Apply system updates and patches across all supported OS
# Compatible: Ansible 2.9.27 and Ansible 6.7.0
# Author: Infrastructure Team
# Date: January 2026
################################################################################

- name: Unified Linux OS Patching
  hosts: all
  become: yes
  gather_facts: yes
  serial: 1  # Patch one host at a time for safety

  vars:
    patch_log_dir: "/var/log/ansible-patching"
    reboot_required_file: "/var/run/reboot-required"
    max_reboot_wait: 600
    pre_patch_snapshot: true

  pre_tasks:
    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    # PRE-FLIGHT CHECKS AND INFORMATION GATHERING
    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    - name: Display execution banner
      debug:
        msg: |
          ========================================
          UNIFIED OS PATCHING PLAYBOOK
          ========================================
          Target Host    : {{ inventory_hostname }}
          OS Family      : {{ ansible_os_family }}
          Distribution   : {{ ansible_distribution }}
          Version        : {{ ansible_distribution_version }}
          Python Version : {{ ansible_python_version }}
          Ansible User   : {{ ansible_user }}
          Become Method  : {{ ansible_become_method }}
          ========================================
      tags: always

    - name: Verify connectivity
      ping:
      tags: always

    - name: Create patch log directory
      file:
        path: "{{ patch_log_dir }}"
        state: directory
        mode: '0755'
        owner: root
        group: root
      tags: always

    - name: Record pre-patch state
      shell: |
        echo "Pre-Patch System State - {{ ansible_date_time.iso8601 }}" > {{ patch_log_dir }}/pre_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Hostname: {{ inventory_hostname }}" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/pre_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Kernel: $(uname -r)" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/pre_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Uptime: $(uptime)" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/pre_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        df -h >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/pre_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
      changed_when: false
      tags: always

  tasks:
    # =========================================================================
    # UBUNTU PATCHING (DEBIAN FAMILY) - Ubuntu 22 and Ubuntu 24
    # =========================================================================
    - name: Ubuntu patching block
      block:
        - name: Update apt cache (Ubuntu)
          apt:
            update_cache: yes
            cache_valid_time: 3600
          tags: patching

        - name: Upgrade all packages to latest version (Ubuntu)
          apt:
            upgrade: dist
            autoremove: yes
            autoclean: yes
          register: apt_upgrade_result
          tags: patching

        - name: Display packages updated (Ubuntu)
          debug:
            msg: "Packages were {{ 'updated' if apt_upgrade_result.changed else 'already up to date' }}"
          tags: patching

        - name: Check if reboot required (Ubuntu)
          stat:
            path: "{{ reboot_required_file }}"
          register: reboot_required_ubuntu
          tags: patching

        - name: Display reboot requirement status (Ubuntu)
          debug:
            msg: "Reboot {{ 'REQUIRED' if reboot_required_ubuntu.stat.exists else 'NOT required' }}"
          tags: patching

      when: ansible_os_family == "Debian"

    # =========================================================================
    # ORACLE LINUX PATCHING (REDHAT FAMILY) - Oracle Linux 8 and 9
    # =========================================================================
    - name: Oracle Linux patching block
      block:
        - name: Update all packages to latest version (Oracle Linux)
          dnf:
            name: "*"
            state: latest
            update_cache: yes
          register: dnf_upgrade_result
          tags: patching

        - name: Display packages updated (Oracle Linux)
          debug:
            msg: "Packages were {{ 'updated' if dnf_upgrade_result.changed else 'already up to date' }}"
          tags: patching

        - name: Check if reboot required (Oracle Linux)
          command: needs-restarting -r
          register: reboot_required_oracle
          failed_when: false
          changed_when: reboot_required_oracle.rc == 1
          tags: patching

        - name: Display reboot requirement status (Oracle Linux)
          debug:
            msg: "Reboot {{ 'REQUIRED' if reboot_required_oracle.changed else 'NOT required' }}"
          tags: patching

      when: ansible_os_family == "RedHat"

    # =========================================================================
    # LOGGING AND DOCUMENTATION
    # =========================================================================
    - name: Log patching results
      copy:
        content: |
          ========================================
          Patching Report for {{ inventory_hostname }}
          ========================================
          Date: {{ ansible_date_time.iso8601 }}
          OS: {{ ansible_distribution }} {{ ansible_distribution_version }}
          OS Family: {{ ansible_os_family }}
          Kernel (pre-patch): {{ ansible_kernel }}
          Python Interpreter: {{ ansible_python_interpreter }}
          
          Package Manager: {{ 'apt' if ansible_os_family == 'Debian' else 'dnf' }}
          Packages Updated: {{ apt_upgrade_result.changed | default(dnf_upgrade_result.changed | default(false)) }}
          
          Reboot Required: {{ reboot_required_ubuntu.stat.exists | default(reboot_required_oracle.changed | default(false)) }}
          
          Ansible Version: {{ ansible_version.string | default('Unknown') }}
          Playbook User: {{ ansible_user }}
          ========================================
        dest: "{{ patch_log_dir }}/patching_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log"
        mode: '0644'
        owner: root
        group: root
      tags: logging

    # =========================================================================
    # REBOOT HANDLING
    # =========================================================================
    - name: Reboot server if required (Ubuntu)
      reboot:
        msg: "Rebooting server after patching - Initiated by Ansible"
        connect_timeout: 5
        reboot_timeout: "{{ max_reboot_wait }}"
        pre_reboot_delay: 0
        post_reboot_delay: 30
        test_command: uptime
      when:
        - ansible_os_family == "Debian"
        - reboot_required_ubuntu.stat.exists is defined
        - reboot_required_ubuntu.stat.exists
        - reboot_after_patch | default(true)
      tags: reboot

    - name: Reboot server if required (Oracle Linux)
      reboot:
        msg: "Rebooting server after patching - Initiated by Ansible"
        connect_timeout: 5
        reboot_timeout: "{{ max_reboot_wait }}"
        pre_reboot_delay: 0
        post_reboot_delay: 30
        test_command: uptime
      when:
        - ansible_os_family == "RedHat"
        - reboot_required_oracle.changed is defined
        - reboot_required_oracle.changed
        - reboot_after_patch | default(true)
      tags: reboot

    - name: Wait for server to come back online after reboot
      wait_for_connection:
        timeout: "{{ max_reboot_wait }}"
        delay: 10
      tags: reboot

    # =========================================================================
    # POST-PATCH VERIFICATION
    # =========================================================================
    - name: Gather facts after patching/reboot
      setup:
      tags: verification

    - name: Verify current kernel version
      command: uname -r
      register: kernel_version
      changed_when: false
      tags: verification

    - name: Display current kernel
      debug:
        msg: "Current kernel: {{ kernel_version.stdout }}"
      tags: verification

    - name: Check disk space after patching
      command: df -h /
      register: disk_space
      changed_when: false
      tags: verification

    - name: Display disk space
      debug:
        msg: "{{ disk_space.stdout_lines }}"
      tags: verification

    - name: Verify critical services are running
      service_facts:
      tags: verification

    - name: Display SSH service status
      debug:
        msg: "SSH service (sshd) is {{ ansible_facts.services['sshd.service'].state | default('unknown') }}"
      tags: verification

  post_tasks:
    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    # FINAL VERIFICATION AND REPORTING
    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    - name: Final connectivity check
      ping:
      tags: always

    - name: Record post-patch state
      shell: |
        echo "Post-Patch System State - {{ ansible_date_time.iso8601 }}" > {{ patch_log_dir }}/post_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Hostname: {{ inventory_hostname }}" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/post_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Kernel: $(uname -r)" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/post_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        echo "Uptime: $(uptime)" >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/post_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
        df -h >> {{ patch_log_dir }}/post_patch_{{ ansible_date_time.date }}.log
      changed_when: false
      tags: always

    - name: Display completion summary
      debug:
        msg: |
          ========================================
          PATCHING COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY
          ========================================
          Host: {{ inventory_hostname }}
          Kernel: {{ kernel_version.stdout }}
          Uptime: {{ ansible_uptime_seconds }} seconds
          Patching Time: {{ ansible_date_time.iso8601 }}
          ========================================
      tags: always
EOF


# Copy to /etc/ansible/playbooks for system Ansible
cp /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml \
   /etc/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml


# Set ownership and permissions
chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks
chmod 644 /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml
chmod 644 /etc/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml


# Verify playbook created
ls -la /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/
ls -la /etc/ansible/playbooks/


PLAYBOOK STRUCTURE EXPLAINED:
------------------------------

PRE_TASKS:
- Display execution information
- Test connectivity
- Create log directories
- Record pre-patch state

MAIN TASKS (OS-Specific):

Ubuntu Block (ansible_os_family == "Debian"):
  - Update apt cache
  - Upgrade all packages (dist-upgrade)
  - Check for reboot requirement file
  
Oracle Linux Block (ansible_os_family == "RedHat"):
  - Update all packages with dnf
  - Check reboot requirement with needs-restarting

LOGGING:
- Create detailed patch report
- Include OS info, package counts, reboot status

REBOOT HANDLING:
- Conditional reboot based on OS detection
- Wait for system to come back online
- Test with uptime command

POST-PATCH VERIFICATION:
- Gather updated facts
- Verify kernel version
- Check disk space
- Verify critical services

POST_TASKS:
- Final connectivity check
- Record post-patch state
- Display completion summary

FEATURES:
- Serial execution (one host at a time)
- OS-agnostic (works on Ubuntu and Oracle Linux)
- Compatible with both Ansible 2.9 and 6.7
- Comprehensive logging
- Automatic reboot handling
- Error handling with failed_when/changed_when
- Tag-based execution (run specific sections)

SECTION 9.2: LEGACY PLAYBOOK (FOR ANSIBLE 2.9 COMPATIBILITY)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create simplified legacy playbook guaranteed to work with Ansible 2.9

EXECUTION: Run commands on control node as root


# Create legacy playbook
cat > /etc/ansible/playbooks/patch_linux_legacy.yml << 'EOF'
---
################################################################################
# LEGACY PLAYBOOK: Linux Patching (Ansible 2.9 Compatible)
# Description: Apply system updates - Simplified legacy format
# Compatible: Ansible 2.9.27
# Use Case: Fallback if unified playbook has issues
################################################################################

- name: Linux Patching (Legacy)
  hosts: all
  become: yes
  serial: 1

  tasks:
    - name: Display target information
      debug:
        msg: "Patching {{ inventory_hostname }} - {{ ansible_distribution }} {{ ansible_distribution_version }}"

    - name: Update all packages (Ubuntu/Debian)
      apt:
        upgrade: dist
        update_cache: yes
        autoremove: yes
      when: ansible_os_family == "Debian"

    - name: Update all packages (RHEL/Oracle)
      yum:
        name: "*"
        state: latest
        update_cache: yes
      when: ansible_os_family == "RedHat"

    - name: Check if reboot required (Debian)
      stat:
        path: /var/run/reboot-required
      register: reboot_required_debian
      when: ansible_os_family == "Debian"

    - name: Check if reboot required (RedHat)
      command: needs-restarting -r
      register: reboot_required_redhat
      failed_when: false
      changed_when: false
      when: ansible_os_family == "RedHat"

    - name: Reboot if required (Debian)
      reboot:
        msg: "Reboot triggered by patching playbook"
        reboot_timeout: 300
      when:
        - ansible_os_family == "Debian"
        - reboot_required_debian.stat.exists is defined
        - reboot_required_debian.stat.exists

    - name: Reboot if required (RedHat)
      reboot:
        msg: "Reboot triggered by patching playbook"
        reboot_timeout: 300
      when:
        - ansible_os_family == "RedHat"
        - reboot_required_redhat.rc is defined
        - reboot_required_redhat.rc == 1

    - name: Wait for connection after reboot
      wait_for_connection:
        timeout: 600

    - name: Verify current kernel
      command: uname -r
      register: kernel_version
      changed_when: false

    - name: Display current kernel
      debug:
        var: kernel_version.stdout

  post_tasks:
    - name: Final summary
      debug:
        msg: "Patch operation completed for {{ inventory_hostname }}"
EOF


# Set permissions
chmod 644 /etc/ansible/playbooks/patch_linux_legacy.yml


LEGACY PLAYBOOK DIFFERENCES:
-----------------------------

1. Simplified structure (no complex blocks)
2. Uses yum instead of dnf (compatible with older systems)
3. Minimal error handling
4. Basic logging only
5. Guaranteed Ansible 2.9 compatibility
6. Use as fallback if unified playbook fails

TROUBLESHOOTING PLAYBOOK ISSUES:
---------------------------------

Issue: "Module not found"
Solution: Verify collections installed in venv
  ansible-galaxy collection list -p ~/ansible-venv/collections

Issue: "Python interpreter not found"
Solution: Verify ansible_python_interpreter in group_vars

Issue: "Permission denied"
Solution: Verify become settings and svc_ans sudo access

Issue: Playbook hangs
Solution: Add -vvv for verbose output to identify stuck task

Issue: "Reboot module not found" (Ansible 2.9)
Solution: Use legacy playbook instead


PLAYBOOK EXECUTION BEST PRACTICES:
-----------------------------------

1. Always run --syntax-check first
2. Always run --check (dry run) before actual execution
3. Test on single host before running on all hosts
4. Use --limit to target specific hosts/groups
5. Use tags to run specific sections
6. Monitor logs in /var/log/ansible-patching/ on targets
7. Keep playbook output for audit trail
8. Schedule patching during maintenance windows
9. Have rollback plan ready
10. Test in non-production environment first

PART 10: JENKINS PIPELINE IMPLEMENTATION
================================================================================

This section configures Jenkins with a production-grade pipeline that:
- Dynamically selects Ansible version based on target OS
- Uses the same playbooks for all OS types
- Supports parameterized execution
- Includes dry-run and approval gates
- Provides comprehensive logging

PREREQUISITES:
- Jenkins installed and running (Part 2 completed)
- Ansible installed (both versions) - Part 6 completed
- Playbooks created - Part 9 completed
- SSH keys configured - Part 5 completed


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 10.1: ADD SSH CREDENTIAL TO JENKINS
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Configure Jenkins to use svc_ans SSH key for Ansible operations

EXECUTION: Perform in Jenkins web UI


Step 1: Get SSH Private Key
----------------------------

# On control node as root
cat /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa

# Expected output:
# -----BEGIN OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----
# b3BlbnNzaC1rZXktdjEAAAAABG5vbmUAAAAEbm9uZQAAAAAAAAABAAACFwAAAAdzc2gtcn
# ... (many lines of encoded key)
# ... 
# -----END OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----


# Copy the ENTIRE output including:
# -----BEGIN OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----
# (all the encoded data)
# -----END OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----


Step 2: Add Credential in Jenkins UI
-------------------------------------

1. Access Jenkins web UI:
   https://jenkinspreprod.local

2. Navigate to:
   Dashboard → Manage Jenkins → Credentials → System → Global credentials (unrestricted)

3. Click: "Add Credentials"

4. Fill in the form:

   Kind: SSH Username with private key
   
   Scope: Global (Jenkins, nodes, items, all child items, etc)
   
   ID: svc_ans_ssh_key
   (IMPORTANT: This ID must match the pipeline script)
   
   Description: svc_ans SSH Private Key for Ansible Automation
   
   Username: svc_ans
   
   Private Key: ☑ Enter directly
   
   Key: Click "Add"
        Paste the entire private key content from Step 1
        (including BEGIN and END lines)
   
   Passphrase: (leave empty - our key has no passphrase)
   
   ID: svc_ans_ssh_key
   
   Description: svc_ans SSH Private Key for Ansible Automation

5. Click: "OK"

6. Verify credential appears in list:
   ID: svc_ans_ssh_key
   Name: svc_ans/****** (svc_ans SSH Private Key for Ansible Automation)


Step 3: Verify Credential
--------------------------

# In Jenkins UI, you should see:
# Credentials → System → Global credentials
#
# ID                  | Name                                      | Kind
# --------------------|-------------------------------------------|------------------
# svc_ans_ssh_key     | svc_ans/****** (svc_ans SSH Private...) | SSH Username with private key


IMPORTANT NOTES:
----------------

1. Credential ID must be exactly: svc_ans_ssh_key
2. This ID is referenced in pipeline script
3. Private key must include BEGIN and END lines
4. No passphrase should be set
5. Scope should be Global for pipeline access


TROUBLESHOOTING:
----------------

Issue: "Credentials not found" in pipeline
Solution: Verify ID matches exactly: svc_ans_ssh_key

Issue: "Authentication failed"
Solution: Verify private key copied correctly (including BEGIN/END lines)

Issue: Pipeline can't access credential
Solution: Verify credential scope is "Global"


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 10.2: PRODUCTION JENKINS PIPELINE (UNIFIED)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Create production-grade Jenkins pipeline with Ansible version selection

EXECUTION: Create new Pipeline job in Jenkins UI


Step 1: Create Pipeline Job
----------------------------

1. In Jenkins UI:
   Dashboard → New Item

2. Configure:
   Enter an item name: Linux-OS-Patching-Unified
   
   Select: Pipeline
   
   Click: OK


Step 2: Configure Pipeline
---------------------------

1. In pipeline configuration page:

   General Section:
   ----------------
   ☑ Discard old builds
     Days to keep builds: 30
     Max # of builds to keep: 30

   ☑ This project is parameterized
     (Parameters will be defined in pipeline script)

   Description:
   "Production OS patching pipeline for Ubuntu 22/24 and Oracle Linux 8/9
    with automatic Ansible version selection"


2. Pipeline Section:
   -----------------
   Definition: Pipeline script

   Script: (paste the following complete pipeline script)


PRODUCTION JENKINS PIPELINE SCRIPT:
------------------------------------

pipeline {
    agent any

    parameters {
        choice(
            name: 'TARGET_GROUP',
            choices: [
                'all_linux',
                'ubuntu',
                'oracle',
                'ubuntu22',
                'ubuntu24',
                'oracle8',
                'oracle9'
            ],
            description: 'Select target group for patching'
        )
        
        choice(
            name: 'ANSIBLE_VERSION',
            choices: ['auto', '2.9', '6.7'],
            description: 'Ansible version (auto-detect based on target, or force specific version)'
        )
        
        booleanParam(
            name: 'DRY_RUN',
            defaultValue: true,
            description: 'Run in check mode (no changes applied)?'
        )
        
        booleanParam(
            name: 'REBOOT_ALLOWED',
            defaultValue: true,
            description: 'Allow automatic reboot if required?'
        )
        
        string(
            name: 'LIMIT_HOSTS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Limit to specific hosts (comma-separated). Leave empty to use TARGET_GROUP.'
        )
        
        string(
            name: 'EXTRA_VARS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Extra variables in format "key1=value1 key2=value2"'
        )
        
        string(
            name: 'TAGS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Ansible tags to run (e.g., patching,verification)'
        )
    }

    environment {
        // Ansible binary paths
        ANSIBLE_29_BIN          = '/usr/bin/ansible'
        ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN = '/usr/bin/ansible-playbook'
        ANSIBLE_67_VENV         = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv'
        ANSIBLE_67_BIN          = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible'
        ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible-playbook'
        
        // Configuration files
        ANSIBLE_29_CFG          = '/etc/ansible/ansible.cfg'
        ANSIBLE_67_CFG          = '/home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg'
        
        // Inventory and playbooks
        ANSIBLE_INVENTORY       = '/home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts'
        PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED        = '/home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml'
        PLAYBOOK_LEGACY         = '/etc/ansible/playbooks/patch_linux_legacy.yml'
        
        // Remote user
        REMOTE_USER             = 'svc_ans'
        
        // Logging
        LOG_DIR                 = '/home/svc_ans/logs'
        BUILD_LOG               = "${LOG_DIR}/jenkins-build-${BUILD_NUMBER}-${BUILD_ID}.log"
    }

    options {
        timestamps()
        buildDiscarder(logRotator(
            numToKeepStr: '30',
            artifactNumToKeepStr: '10',
            daysToKeepStr: '90'
        ))
        timeout(time: 3, unit: 'HOURS')
        disableConcurrentBuilds()
        ansiColor('xterm')
    }

    stages {

        stage('Environment Validation') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        JENKINS ANSIBLE PIPELINE
                        ============================================
                        Build Number    : ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
                        Build ID        : ${env.BUILD_ID}
                        Target Group    : ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
                        Ansible Version : ${params.ANSIBLE_VERSION}
                        Dry Run         : ${params.DRY_RUN}
                        Reboot Allowed  : ${params.REBOOT_ALLOWED}
                        Limit Hosts     : ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: 'None (use TARGET_GROUP)'}
                        Extra Vars      : ${params.EXTRA_VARS ?: 'None'}
                        Tags            : ${params.TAGS ?: 'All'}
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        echo "Validating environment..."
                        
                        # Validate required files exist
                        [ -f "${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}" ]      || { echo "ERROR: Ansible 2.9 binary missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -d "${ANSIBLE_67_VENV}" ]     || { echo "ERROR: Ansible 6.7 venv missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY}" ]   || { echo "ERROR: Inventory missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}" ]    || { echo "ERROR: Unified playbook missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${SSH_KEY}" ]             || { echo "ERROR: SSH key not injected"; exit 1; }
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "--- System Ansible 2.9 ---"
                        ${ANSIBLE_29_BIN} --version | head -5
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "--- Virtual Environment Ansible 6.7 ---"
                        ${ANSIBLE_67_BIN} --version | head -5
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "--- Inventory Hosts for ${TARGET_GROUP} ---"
                        ${ANSIBLE_29_BIN} -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} --list-hosts ${TARGET_GROUP}
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Environment validation PASSED"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Connectivity Test') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        TESTING CONNECTIVITY TO TARGET HOSTS
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        # Determine which Ansible version to use
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "6.7" ] || [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 6.7 from virtual environment"
                        elif [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 2.9 from system (forced)"
                        else
                            # Auto-detect based on target group
                            if [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                                echo "Using Ansible 6.7 (auto-detected for ubuntu24)"
                            else
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                                echo "Using Ansible 2.9 (auto-detected)"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "Testing connectivity with ping module..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m ping \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Connectivity test PASSED"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Pre-Patch Information') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        GATHERING PRE-PATCH INFORMATION
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        # Determine Ansible version
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "6.7" ] || [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                        elif [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                        else
                            if [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            else
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        echo "Current system state (kernel, uptime, disk):"
                        echo ""
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m shell \
                            -a "echo 'Host: '\\$(hostname) && echo 'Kernel: '\\$(uname -r) && echo 'Uptime: '\\$(uptime | cut -d',' -f1) && echo 'Disk:' && df -h / | tail -1" \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Dry Run') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == true }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        EXECUTING DRY RUN (CHECK MODE)
                        NO CHANGES WILL BE APPLIED
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        # Determine Ansible version and playbook
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "6.7" ] || [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                            echo "Executing with Ansible 6.7 (venv)"
                        elif [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                            echo "Executing with Ansible 2.9 (system - forced)"
                        else
                            if [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                                ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                                PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                                echo "Executing with Ansible 6.7 (auto-detected for ubuntu24)"
                            else
                                ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                                PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                                echo "Executing with Ansible 2.9 (auto-detected)"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        # Build limit parameter
                        if [ -n "${LIMIT_HOSTS}" ]; then
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                            echo "Limiting to hosts: ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                        else
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                            echo "Limiting to group: ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                        fi
                        
                        # Build extra vars parameter
                        EXTRA_VARS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS}" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_PARAM="-e '${EXTRA_VARS}'"
                            echo "Extra variables: ${EXTRA_VARS}"
                        fi
                        
                        # Build tags parameter
                        TAGS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${TAGS}" ]; then
                            TAGS_PARAM="-t ${TAGS}"
                            echo "Running tags: ${TAGS}"
                        fi
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "Executing dry run..."
                        
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            ${PLAYBOOK} \
                            ${LIMIT_PARAM} \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER} \
                            ${EXTRA_VARS_PARAM} \
                            ${TAGS_PARAM} \
                            --check \
                            --diff \
                            -v
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Dry run completed successfully"
                        echo "Review output above to verify expected changes"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Approval for Production') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == false }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    def targetInfo = params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP
                    
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        PRODUCTION EXECUTION APPROVAL REQUIRED
                        ============================================
                        Target: ${targetInfo}
                        This will apply actual changes to systems.
                        Reboot: ${params.REBOOT_ALLOWED ? 'ALLOWED' : 'DISABLED'}
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                timeout(time: 30, unit: 'MINUTES') {
                    input(
                        message: "Proceed with actual patching on ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP}?",
                        ok: 'Yes, Execute Patching',
                        submitter: 'authenticated'
                    )
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Execute Patching') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == false }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        EXECUTING PRODUCTION OS PATCHING
                        Target: ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP}
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        # Determine Ansible version and playbook
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "6.7" ] || [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                            echo "Executing with Ansible 6.7"
                        elif [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                            echo "Executing with Ansible 2.9 (forced)"
                        else
                            if [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                                ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                                PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                                echo "Executing with Ansible 6.7 (auto)"
                            else
                                ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                                PLAYBOOK="${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                                echo "Executing with Ansible 2.9 (auto)"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        # Build limit parameter
                        if [ -n "${LIMIT_HOSTS}" ]; then
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                        else
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                        fi
                        
                        # Build extra vars
                        EXTRA_VARS_BUILD=""
                        if [ "${REBOOT_ALLOWED}" = "false" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_BUILD="reboot_after_patch=false"
                        fi
                        
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS}" ]; then
                            if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD}" ]; then
                                EXTRA_VARS_BUILD="${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD} ${EXTRA_VARS}"
                            else
                                EXTRA_VARS_BUILD="${EXTRA_VARS}"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        EXTRA_VARS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD}" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_PARAM="-e '${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD}'"
                        fi
                        
                        # Build tags parameter
                        TAGS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${TAGS}" ]; then
                            TAGS_PARAM="-t ${TAGS}"
                        fi
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "Executing production patching..."
                        echo "Playbook: ${PLAYBOOK}"
                        echo "Limit: ${LIMIT_PARAM}"
                        echo "Extra Vars: ${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD:-None}"
                        echo ""
                        
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            ${PLAYBOOK} \
                            ${LIMIT_PARAM} \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER} \
                            ${EXTRA_VARS_PARAM} \
                            ${TAGS_PARAM} \
                            -v
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Production patching completed"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        stage('Post-Patch Verification') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
                        ============================================
                        POST-PATCH VERIFICATION
                        ============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        # Determine Ansible version
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "6.7" ] || [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                        elif [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                        else
                            if [ "${TARGET_GROUP}" = "ubuntu24" ]; then
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            else
                                ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                                ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            fi
                        fi
                        
                        echo "Verifying all hosts are accessible..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m ping \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "Checking post-patch state (kernel, uptime)..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m shell \
                            -a "echo '=== '\\$(hostname)' ===' && echo 'Kernel: '\\$(uname -r) && echo 'Uptime: '\\$(uptime | cut -d',' -f1) && echo 'Last Boot: '\\$(who -b | awk '{print \\$3,\\$4}')" \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}
                        
                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Post-patch verification completed"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }
    }

    post {
        success {
            script {
                echo """
                    ============================================
                    ✓ PATCHING COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY
                    ============================================
                    Build Number: ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
                    Target Group: ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
                    Ansible Version: ${params.ANSIBLE_VERSION}
                    Dry Run: ${params.DRY_RUN}
                    Duration: ${currentBuild.durationString}
                    ============================================
                """.stripIndent()
            }
        }
        
        failure {
            script {
                echo """
                    ============================================
                    ✗ PATCHING FAILED
                    ============================================
                    Build Number: ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
                    Target Group: ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
                    Check logs above for error details
                    ============================================
                """.stripIndent()
            }
        }
        
        always {
            script {
                echo """
                    ============================================
                    PIPELINE EXECUTION SUMMARY
                    ============================================
                    Job: ${env.JOB_NAME}
                    Build: ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
                    Status: ${currentBuild.currentResult}
                    Duration: ${currentBuild.durationString}
                    Started: ${new Date(currentBuild.startTimeInMillis).format('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')}
                    ============================================
                """.stripIndent()
                
                // Archive wrapper logs if they exist
                sh '''
                    if [ -d "${LOG_DIR}" ]; then
                        find ${LOG_DIR} -type f -name "wrapper_*.log" -mtime -1 -exec cp {} ${WORKSPACE}/ \\; 2>/dev/null || true
                    fi
                '''
                
                archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'wrapper_*.log', allowEmptyArchive: true
            }
        }
    }
}

  Jenkins User    : jenkins (uid=994, gid=991)
  Ansible User    : svc_ans
  Credential ID   : svc_ans_ssh_key (SSH private key in Jenkins)

  Target Hosts:
  ┌─────────────────────┬──────────────────┬────────────┬───────────────────┐
