SECTION 2 — IPTABLES FIXES
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2a. jesus-VMware-Virtual-Platform
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Issues Found:
  - SSH open to world (0.0.0.0/0 tcp dpt:22) — no source restriction
  - Redundant rule: ACCEPT from 192.168.121.182 tcp dpt:22 (covered by above)
  - No SSH brute-force rate limiting
  - No iptables-persistent installed

Actions Taken:
  iptables -P INPUT DROP
  iptables -P FORWARD DROP
  apt install iptables-persistent -y
  netfilter-persistent save

Recommended (pending):
  # Remove world-open SSH, restrict to subnet
  iptables -R INPUT 3 -s 192.168.121.0/24 -p tcp --dport 22 -j ACCEPT
  iptables -D INPUT 4

  # Add brute-force protection
  iptables -I INPUT 3 -p tcp --dport 22 -m state --state NEW -m recent --set
  iptables -I INPUT 4 -p tcp --dport 22 -m state --state NEW -m recent \
      --update --seconds 60 --hitcount 4 -j DROP

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2b. IPv6 — Disabled System-Wide
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  ip6tables -F
  ip6tables -X
  ip6tables -Z
  ip6tables -P INPUT ACCEPT
  ip6tables -P FORWARD ACCEPT
  ip6tables -P OUTPUT ACCEPT

  echo "net.ipv6.conf.all.disable_ipv6 = 1"     >> /etc/sysctl.conf
  echo "net.ipv6.conf.default.disable_ipv6 = 1" >> /etc/sysctl.conf
  echo "net.ipv6.conf.lo.disable_ipv6 = 1"      >> /etc/sysctl.conf
  sysctl -p
  netfilter-persistent save

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
2c. ubuntu24 (192.168.121.164) — Rebuilt from Scratch
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Issues Found:
  - INPUT policy was ACCEPT (should be DROP) — all rules were redundant
  - Duplicate ruleset after netfilter-persistent save (every rule appeared twice)
  - LOG rule logging all traffic, not just drops

Fix — full flush and clean rebuild:
  iptables -F && iptables -X && iptables -Z
  iptables -P INPUT DROP
  iptables -P FORWARD DROP
  iptables -P OUTPUT ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -i lo -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -m state --state RELATED,ESTABLISHED -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -p tcp --dport 22 -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -p tcp --dport 443 -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -p icmp --icmp-type echo-request -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -p icmp --icmp-type echo-reply -j ACCEPT
  iptables -A INPUT -j LOG --log-prefix "IPTABLES-DROP: " --log-level 4
  netfilter-persistent save


════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 3 — ANSIBLE FIXES
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
3a. svc_ans Venv — /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Problem 1: community.general version conflict
  community.general 12.6.1 in ~/.ansible/collections  ← incompatible with 2.13
  community.general  5.8.3 in /usr/share/ansible       ← compatible
  Fix:
    rm -rf ~/.ansible/collections/ansible_collections/community/general
    ansible-galaxy collection install community.general:==5.8.3 --force

Problem 2: stdout_callback redirecting to removed community.general.yaml plugin
  Fix in /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg:
    stdout_callback = ansible.builtin.default
    result_format   = yaml

Problem 3: control_path incompatible with Python % string formatter
  Error: ValueError: unsupported format character '-' (0x2d) at index 19
  Root cause: SSH tokens %h %p %r separated by dashes — Python sees %-h as
              invalid % format specifier
  Bad:  control_path = /tmp/ansible-ssh-%h-%p-%r
  Fix:  control_path = %(directory)s/%%h-%%p-%%r

Problem 4: private_key_file hardcoded — caused Jenkins SSH permission failure
  Fix:
    sed -i '/private_key_file/d' /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg

Final /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg [defaults] section:
  inventory          = /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts
  remote_user        = svc_ans
  host_key_checking  = False
  interpreter_python = auto_silent
  stdout_callback    = ansible.builtin.default
  result_format      = yaml
  bin_ansible_callbacks = True
  log_path           = /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log
  collections_paths  = /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/collections:/home/svc_ans/.ansible/collections

  [ssh_connection]
  pipelining   = True
  control_path = %(directory)s/%%h-%%p-%%r

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
3b. root System Ansible — /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Problem 1: Same bad control_path
  sed -i 's|control_path = /tmp/ansible-ssh-%h-%p-%r|control_path = %(directory)s/%%h-%%p-%%r|' \
      /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg

Problem 2: Ansible 2.9 + Python 3.12 = incompatible (ubuntu24 target)
  Error: ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'ansible.module_utils.six.moves'
  Root cause: Ansible 2.9 bundles its own six module which is broken on Python 3.12
  Fix: Redirect root to use the venv binary
    echo 'export PATH=/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin:$PATH' >> /root/.bashrc
    echo 'export PATH=/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin:$PATH' >> /root/.bash_profile
    source /root/.bashrc

Recommended (pending):
  yum remove ansible -y   # remove EOL system Ansible 2.9 entirely


════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 4 — JENKINS FIXES
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
4a. AnsiColor Plugin Missing
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Error:
  Invalid option type "ansiColor". Valid option types: [...]  @ line 90

Fix:
  Manage Jenkins → Plugins → Available plugins → AnsiColor → Install + Restart
  Or manually on Jenkins server:
    cd /var/lib/jenkins/plugins
    wget https://updates.jenkins.io/latest/ansicolor.hpi
    chown jenkins:jenkins ansicolor.hpi
    systemctl restart jenkins

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
4b. Pipeline Build 3 — Environment Validation Failure
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Error:
  ansible: error: the following arguments are required: pattern

Root cause:
  Jenkinsfile was calling:
    ${ANSIBLE_29_BIN} -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} --list-hosts ${TARGET_GROUP}
  Ansible 2.9 requires the host pattern BEFORE flags, and used wrong binary.

Fix:
  ${ANSIBLE_67_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} --list-hosts

Additional Jenkinsfile fixes in same revision:
  - Added ANSIBLE_CONFIG = '/home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg' to environment block
  - Simplified version-selection: 6.7 venv for all, except when 2.9 forced
  - Eliminated copy-pasted if/elif/else version blocks across 5 stages
  - Removed unused PLAYBOOK_LEGACY variable
  - Fixed EXTRA_VARS_PARAM shell quoting

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
4c. Pipeline Builds 4 & 5 — SSH Key Permission Denied (all hosts)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Error:
  load pubkey "/home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa": Permission denied
  no such identity: /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa: Permission denied

Root cause:
  - Jenkins runs as: jenkins (uid=994, gid=991)
  - id_rsa was: -rw------- svc_ans:svc_ans (jenkins had zero access)
  - ansible.cfg had: private_key_file = /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
  - SSH loaded ansible.cfg first and tried to read that file → Permission denied
  - The withCredentials injected ${SSH_KEY} temp file was fine, but ansible.cfg
    forced a second key load that jenkins could not read

Fixes Applied:
  # SSH directory and key permissions
  chown svc_ans:jenkins /home/svc_ans/.ssh
  chmod 750 /home/svc_ans/.ssh
  chown svc_ans:jenkins /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
  chmod 640 /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa

  # Log file permissions
  touch /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log
  chown jenkins:jenkins /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log
  chmod 664 /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log

  # Remove hardcoded key from ansible.cfg
  sed -i '/private_key_file/d' /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg

Verification:
  sudo -u jenkins cat /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa > /dev/null && echo "OK"
  → OK

Final permissions:
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/            drwxr-x---  svc_ans:jenkins
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa      -rw-r-----  svc_ans:jenkins
  /home/svc_ans/logs/ansible.log -rw-rw-r--  jenkins:jenkins


════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 5 — FINAL JENKINSFILE
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

pipeline {
    agent any

    parameters {
        choice(
            name: 'TARGET_GROUP',
            choices: [
                'all_linux',
                'ubuntu',
                'oracle',
                'ubuntu22',
                'ubuntu24',
                'oracle8',
                'oracle9'
            ],
            description: 'Select target group for patching'
        )

        choice(
            name: 'ANSIBLE_VERSION',
            choices: ['auto', '2.9', '6.7'],
            description: 'Ansible version: auto uses 6.7 venv for all Ubuntu, 2.9 for Oracle only. Force overrides.'
        )

        booleanParam(
            name: 'DRY_RUN',
            defaultValue: true,
            description: 'Run in check mode (no changes applied)?'
        )

        booleanParam(
            name: 'REBOOT_ALLOWED',
            defaultValue: true,
            description: 'Allow automatic reboot if required?'
        )

        string(
            name: 'LIMIT_HOSTS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Limit to specific hosts (comma-separated). Leave empty to use TARGET_GROUP.'
        )

        string(
            name: 'EXTRA_VARS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Extra variables in format "key1=value1 key2=value2"'
        )

        string(
            name: 'TAGS',
            defaultValue: '',
            description: 'Optional: Ansible tags to run (e.g., patching,verification)'
        )
    }

    environment {
        ANSIBLE_29_BIN          = '/usr/bin/ansible'
        ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN = '/usr/bin/ansible-playbook'
        ANSIBLE_67_VENV         = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv'
        ANSIBLE_67_BIN          = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible'
        ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN = '/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible-playbook'
        ANSIBLE_29_CFG          = '/etc/ansible/ansible.cfg'
        ANSIBLE_67_CFG          = '/home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg'
        ANSIBLE_CONFIG          = '/home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg'
        ANSIBLE_INVENTORY       = '/home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts'
        PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED        = '/home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/os_patching_unified.yml'
        REMOTE_USER             = 'svc_ans'
        LOG_DIR                 = '/home/svc_ans/logs'
    }

    options {
        timestamps()
        buildDiscarder(logRotator(
            numToKeepStr: '30',
            artifactNumToKeepStr: '10',
            daysToKeepStr: '90'
        ))
        timeout(time: 3, unit: 'HOURS')
        disableConcurrentBuilds()
        ansiColor('xterm')
    }

    stages {

        // STAGE 1: Environment Validation
        stage('Environment Validation') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
JENKINS ANSIBLE PIPELINE
============================================
Build Number    : ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
Build ID        : ${env.BUILD_ID}
Target Group    : ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
Ansible Version : ${params.ANSIBLE_VERSION}
Dry Run         : ${params.DRY_RUN}
Reboot Allowed  : ${params.REBOOT_ALLOWED}
Limit Hosts     : ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: 'None (use TARGET_GROUP)'}
Extra Vars      : ${params.EXTRA_VARS ?: 'None'}
Tags            : ${params.TAGS ?: 'All'}
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        echo "Validating environment..."
                        [ -f "${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}" ]      || { echo "ERROR: Ansible 2.9 binary missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -d "${ANSIBLE_67_VENV}" ]     || { echo "ERROR: Ansible 6.7 venv missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}" ]      || { echo "ERROR: Ansible 6.7 binary missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY}" ]   || { echo "ERROR: Inventory missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}" ]    || { echo "ERROR: Unified playbook missing"; exit 1; }
                        [ -f "${SSH_KEY}" ]             || { echo "ERROR: SSH key not injected"; exit 1; }

                        echo ""
                        echo "--- System Ansible 2.9 ---"
                        ${ANSIBLE_29_BIN} --version | head -3

                        echo ""
                        echo "--- Virtual Environment Ansible 6.7 ---"
                        ${ANSIBLE_67_BIN} --version | head -3

                        echo ""
                        echo "--- Inventory Hosts for ${TARGET_GROUP} ---"
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_67_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_67_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            --list-hosts

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Environment validation PASSED"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 2: Connectivity Test
        stage('Connectivity Test') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
TESTING CONNECTIVITY TO TARGET HOSTS
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 2.9 (forced)"
                        else
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 6.7 venv (version: ${ANSIBLE_VERSION})"
                        fi

                        echo ""
                        echo "Testing connectivity with ping module..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m ping \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Connectivity test PASSED"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 3: Pre-Patch Information
        stage('Pre-Patch Information') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
GATHERING PRE-PATCH INFORMATION
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                        else
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                        fi

                        echo "Current system state (kernel, uptime, disk):"
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m shell \
                            -a "echo 'Host: '$(hostname) && \
                                echo 'Kernel: '$(uname -r) && \
                                echo 'Uptime: '$(uptime | cut -d',' -f1) && \
                                echo 'Disk:' && df -h / | tail -1" \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Pre-patch information gathered"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 4: Dry Run
        stage('Dry Run') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == true }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
EXECUTING DRY RUN (CHECK MODE)
NO CHANGES WILL BE APPLIED
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 2.9 (forced)"
                        else
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 6.7 venv"
                        fi

                        if [ -n "${LIMIT_HOSTS}" ]; then
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                            echo "Limiting to hosts: ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                        else
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                            echo "Targeting group: ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                        fi

                        EXTRA_VARS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS}" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_PARAM="-e ${EXTRA_VARS}"
                            echo "Extra variables: ${EXTRA_VARS}"
                        fi

                        TAGS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${TAGS}" ]; then
                            TAGS_PARAM="-t ${TAGS}"
                            echo "Running tags: ${TAGS}"
                        fi

                        echo ""
                        echo "Executing dry run..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            ${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED} \
                            ${LIMIT_PARAM} \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER} \
                            ${EXTRA_VARS_PARAM} \
                            ${TAGS_PARAM} \
                            --check \
                            --diff \
                            -v

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Dry run completed — review output above before proceeding"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 5: Approval Gate (production only)
        stage('Approval for Production') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == false }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    def targetInfo = params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP
                    echo """
============================================
PRODUCTION EXECUTION APPROVAL REQUIRED
============================================
Target  : ${targetInfo}
Reboot  : ${params.REBOOT_ALLOWED ? 'ALLOWED' : 'DISABLED'}
This will apply REAL changes to production systems.
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                timeout(time: 30, unit: 'MINUTES') {
                    input(
                        message: "Proceed with actual patching on ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP}?",
                        ok: 'Yes, Execute Patching',
                        submitter: 'authenticated'
                    )
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 6: Execute Patching (production only)
        stage('Execute Patching') {
            when {
                expression { params.DRY_RUN == false }
            }
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
EXECUTING PRODUCTION OS PATCHING
Target: ${params.LIMIT_HOSTS ?: params.TARGET_GROUP}
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 2.9 (forced)"
                        else
                            ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_PLAYBOOK_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                            echo "Using Ansible 6.7 venv"
                        fi

                        if [ -n "${LIMIT_HOSTS}" ]; then
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${LIMIT_HOSTS}"
                        else
                            LIMIT_PARAM="--limit ${TARGET_GROUP}"
                        fi

                        EXTRA_VARS_BUILD=""
                        if [ "${REBOOT_ALLOWED}" = "false" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_BUILD="reboot_after_patch=false"
                        fi
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS}" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_BUILD="${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD:+${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD} }${EXTRA_VARS}"
                        fi
                        EXTRA_VARS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD}" ]; then
                            EXTRA_VARS_PARAM="-e ${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD}"
                        fi

                        TAGS_PARAM=""
                        if [ -n "${TAGS}" ]; then
                            TAGS_PARAM="-t ${TAGS}"
                        fi

                        echo ""
                        echo "Playbook  : ${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED}"
                        echo "Limit     : ${LIMIT_PARAM}"
                        echo "Extra Vars: ${EXTRA_VARS_BUILD:-None}"
                        echo ""

                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_PLAYBOOK_BIN} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            ${PLAYBOOK_UNIFIED} \
                            ${LIMIT_PARAM} \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER} \
                            ${EXTRA_VARS_PARAM} \
                            ${TAGS_PARAM} \
                            -v

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Production patching completed"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }

        // STAGE 7: Post-Patch Verification
        stage('Post-Patch Verification') {
            steps {
                script {
                    echo """
============================================
POST-PATCH VERIFICATION
============================================
                    """.stripIndent()
                }
                withCredentials([sshUserPrivateKey(
                    credentialsId: 'svc_ans_ssh_key',
                    keyFileVariable: 'SSH_KEY'
                )]) {
                    sh '''
                        if [ "${ANSIBLE_VERSION}" = "2.9" ]; then
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_29_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_29_CFG}"
                        else
                            ANSIBLE_BIN="${ANSIBLE_67_BIN}"
                            ANSIBLE_CFG="${ANSIBLE_67_CFG}"
                        fi

                        echo "Verifying all hosts are accessible..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m ping \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}

                        echo ""
                        echo "Post-patch system state (kernel, uptime, last boot)..."
                        ANSIBLE_CONFIG=${ANSIBLE_CFG} ${ANSIBLE_BIN} ${TARGET_GROUP} \
                            -i ${ANSIBLE_INVENTORY} \
                            -m shell \
                            -a "echo '=== '$(hostname)' ===' && \
                                echo 'Kernel: '$(uname -r) && \
                                echo 'Uptime: '$(uptime | cut -d',' -f1) && \
                                echo 'Last Boot: '$(who -b | awk '{print \$3,\$4}')" \
                            --private-key ${SSH_KEY} \
                            -u ${REMOTE_USER}

                        echo ""
                        echo "✓ Post-patch verification completed"
                    '''
                }
            }
        }
    }

    post {
        success {
            script {
                echo """
============================================
✓ PATCHING COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY
============================================
Build Number  : ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
Target Group  : ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
Ansible Vers  : ${params.ANSIBLE_VERSION}
Dry Run       : ${params.DRY_RUN}
Duration      : ${currentBuild.durationString}
============================================
                """.stripIndent()
            }
        }

        failure {
            script {
                echo """
============================================
✗ PATCHING FAILED
============================================
Build Number  : ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
Target Group  : ${params.TARGET_GROUP}
Check logs above for error details
============================================
                """.stripIndent()
            }
        }

        always {
            script {
                echo """
============================================
PIPELINE EXECUTION SUMMARY
============================================
Job     : ${env.JOB_NAME}
Build   : ${env.BUILD_NUMBER}
Status  : ${currentBuild.currentResult}
Duration: ${currentBuild.durationString}
Started : ${new Date(currentBuild.startTimeInMillis).format('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')}
============================================
                """.stripIndent()

                sh '''
                    if [ -d "${LOG_DIR}" ]; then
                        find ${LOG_DIR} -type f -name "wrapper_*.log" -mtime -1 \
                            -exec cp {} ${WORKSPACE}/ \\; 2>/dev/null || true
                    fi
                '''

                archiveArtifacts artifacts: 'wrapper_*.log', allowEmptyArchive: true
            }
        }
    }
}

        iptables -I INPUT 3 -p tcp --dport 22 -m state --state NEW -m recent --set

            --update --seconds 60 --hitcount 4 -j DROP

Step 3: Save Pipeline

Click: "Save"


PIPELINE CONFIGURATION COMPLETE
================================

The Jenkins pipeline is now configured with:

✓ Parameterized execution
✓ Automatic Ansible version selection
✓ Dry-run capability
✓ Production approval gate
✓ Comprehensive validation stages
✓ Post-patch verification
✓ Logging and artifact archival


TESTING THE PIPELINE
====================

Test 1: Dry Run on Ubuntu 22
-----------------------------

1. In Jenkins UI, navigate to: Linux-OS-Patching-Unified
2. Click: "Build with Parameters"
3. Set parameters:
   - TARGET_GROUP: ubuntu22
   - ANSIBLE_VERSION: auto
   - DRY_RUN: true
   - REBOOT_ALLOWED: true
   - (leave others empty)
4. Click: "Build"
5. Monitor console output
6. Verify: Dry Run stage completes successfully


Test 2: Dry Run on Ubuntu 24
-----------------------------

1. Click: "Build with Parameters"
2. Set parameters:
   - TARGET_GROUP: ubuntu24
   - ANSIBLE_VERSION: auto
   - DRY_RUN: true
   - REBOOT_ALLOWED: true
3. Click: "Build"
4. Verify: Uses Ansible 6.7 from venv


Test 3: Production Run (Single Host)
-------------------------------------

1. Click: "Build with Parameters"
2. Set parameters:
   - TARGET_GROUP: ubuntu22
   - ANSIBLE_VERSION: auto
   - DRY_RUN: false
   - REBOOT_ALLOWED: true
   - LIMIT_HOSTS: 192.168.68.110
3. Click: "Build"
4. Wait for approval prompt
5. Click: "Yes, Execute Patching"
6. Verify: Build completes successfully

================================================================================
PART 11 : LDAP INTEGRATION
================================================================================

Document Purpose:
-----------------
This section provides enterprise-grade LDAP/Active Directory integration
configuration for Jenkins running on Oracle Linux 8.

Environment:
------------
Jenkins URL : https://jenkinspreprod.local
Jenkins Ver : 2.479.2 LTS
LDAP Plugin : Latest Stable
Security     : HTTPS + LDAP Authentication

Objectives:
-----------
- Integrate Jenkins with LDAP / Active Directory
- Centralized authentication
- Role-based authorization
- Restrict anonymous access
- Improve enterprise security posture
- Enable production-grade access control

Supported LDAP Types:
---------------------
- OpenLDAP
- Microsoft Active Directory
- Red Hat IDM / FreeIPA
- Oracle Directory Server

================================================================================
SECTION 11.1 : INSTALL LDAP PLUGIN
================================================================================

PURPOSE:
--------
Install LDAP plugin into Jenkins to enable centralized authentication.

STEP 1: LOGIN TO JENKINS
-------------------------

Open browser:
    https://jenkinspreprod.local

Login with:
    Jenkins local admin account

Example:
    admin / ********

================================================================================
STEP 2: OPEN PLUGIN MANAGER
================================================================================

Navigate:
    Dashboard
      ->
    Manage Jenkins
      ->
    Plugins

================================================================================
STEP 3: INSTALL LDAP PLUGIN
================================================================================

Click:
    Available Plugins

Search:
    LDAP

Expected Plugin:
    LDAP Plugin

Publisher:
    Jenkins Community

Description:
    Adds LDAP authentication support to Jenkins.

================================================================================
STEP 4: INSTALL
================================================================================

Select:
    LDAP Plugin

Click:
    Install

Recommended:
    Select:
        Restart Jenkins when installation is complete
    OR
        Install without restart
        Then restart manually later

================================================================================
STEP 5: VERIFY INSTALLATION
================================================================================

Navigate:
    Manage Jenkins
      ->
    Plugins
      ->
    Installed Plugins

Search:
    LDAP

Expected:
    LDAP Plugin listed as Installed

================================================================================
OPTIONAL COMMAND-LINE VERIFICATION
================================================================================

Check Jenkins plugins directory:

    ls -la /var/lib/jenkins/plugins | grep ldap

Expected:
    ldap.jpi

================================================================================
RESTART JENKINS (IF REQUIRED)
================================================================================

systemctl restart jenkins

Verify:
    systemctl status jenkins

================================================================================
SECTION 11.2 : CONFIGURE LDAP SECURITY REALM
================================================================================

PURPOSE:
--------
Configure Jenkins authentication using enterprise LDAP/Active Directory.

================================================================================
STEP 1: OPEN SECURITY CONFIGURATION
================================================================================

Navigate:
    Dashboard
      ->
    Manage Jenkins
      ->
    Security

================================================================================
STEP 2: ENABLE SECURITY
================================================================================

Enable:
    [✓] Enable Security

================================================================================
STEP 3: SELECT SECURITY REALM
================================================================================

Under:
    Security Realm

Select:
    LDAP

================================================================================
STEP 4: ENTER LDAP CONFIGURATION
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A) STANDARD OPENLDAP EXAMPLE
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server:
    ldap://ldap.example.com:389

OR Secure LDAP:
    ldaps://ldap.example.com:636

Root DN:
    dc=example,dc=com

User Search Base:
    ou=users

User Search Filter:
    uid={0}

Group Search Base:
    ou=groups

Manager DN:
    cn=ldap-reader,ou=service,dc=example,dc=com

Manager Password:
    ********

Display Name LDAP Attribute:
    cn

Email Address LDAP Attribute:
    mail

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
B) MICROSOFT ACTIVE DIRECTORY EXAMPLE
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server:
    ldap://ad.company.local:389

OR Secure:
    ldaps://ad.company.local:636

Root DN:
    dc=company,dc=local

User Search Base:
    ou=Employees

User Search Filter:
    sAMAccountName={0}

Group Search Base:
    ou=Groups

Manager DN:
    cn=svc_jenkins,ou=ServiceAccounts,dc=company,dc=local

Manager Password:
    ********

Display Name LDAP Attribute:
    displayName

Email Address LDAP Attribute:
    mail

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
C) FREEIPA / IDM EXAMPLE
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server:
    ldap://idm.company.local:389

Root DN:
    dc=company,dc=local

User Search Base:
    cn=users,cn=accounts

User Search Filter:
    uid={0}

Group Search Base:
    cn=groups,cn=accounts

Manager DN:
    uid=svc_jenkins,cn=users,cn=accounts,dc=company,dc=local

Manager Password:
    ********

================================================================================
FIELD EXPLANATION
================================================================================

Server:
--------
LDAP server hostname and port.

Port 389:
    Standard LDAP

Port 636:
    Secure LDAP (LDAPS)

Recommendation:
    Use LDAPS in production.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Root DN
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Base directory where searches begin.

Example:
    dc=company,dc=local

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
User Search Base
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Location of user accounts.

Examples:
    ou=Employees
    ou=Users

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
User Search Filter
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Defines username lookup attribute.

OpenLDAP:
    uid={0}

Active Directory:
    sAMAccountName={0}

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Manager DN
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LDAP bind account used by Jenkins.

Recommendation:
    Create read-only LDAP service account.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Display Name Attribute
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LDAP field shown in Jenkins UI.

Common:
    cn
    displayName

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Email Address Attribute
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Used for Jenkins notifications.

Common:
    mail

================================================================================
SECTION 11.3 : TEST LDAP CONNECTION
================================================================================

PURPOSE:
--------
Validate LDAP connectivity and user authentication before saving.

================================================================================
METHOD 1 : JENKINS UI TEST
================================================================================

In Jenkins Security Page:

Click:
    Test LDAP Settings

Enter:
    Username
    Password

Example:
    jdoe
    ********

Expected:
    Authentication Successful

Expected Details:
    User DN:
    cn=jdoe,ou=Employees,dc=company,dc=local

================================================================================
METHOD 2 : COMMAND-LINE LDAP TEST
================================================================================

Install LDAP client tools:

Oracle Linux:
--------------
dnf install -y openldap-clients

Ubuntu:
--------
apt install -y ldap-utils

================================================================================
TEST LDAP SEARCH
================================================================================

ldapsearch -x \
-H ldap://ldap.example.com:389 \
-D "cn=ldap-reader,ou=service,dc=example,dc=com" \
-W \
-b "dc=example,dc=com"

Expected:
    LDAP entries returned

================================================================================
ACTIVE DIRECTORY TEST
================================================================================

ldapsearch -x \
-H ldap://ad.company.local:389 \
-D "cn=svc_jenkins,ou=ServiceAccounts,dc=company,dc=local" \
-W \
-b "dc=company,dc=local"

================================================================================
TEST SPECIFIC USER
================================================================================

ldapsearch -x \
-H ldap://ldap.example.com:389 \
-D "cn=ldap-reader,ou=service,dc=example,dc=com" \
-W \
-b "dc=example,dc=com" \
"(uid=jdoe)"

Expected:
    User object returned

================================================================================
NETWORK CONNECTIVITY TEST
================================================================================

telnet ldap.example.com 389

OR

nc -zv ldap.example.com 389

Expected:
    Connection successful

================================================================================
TLS/SSL LDAP TEST
================================================================================

openssl s_client -connect ldap.example.com:636

Expected:
    Certificate chain displayed

================================================================================
SECTION 11.4 : AUTHORIZATION STRATEGY
================================================================================

PURPOSE:
--------
Define what authenticated LDAP users can access inside Jenkins.

================================================================================
OPTION 1 : LOGGED-IN USERS CAN DO ANYTHING
================================================================================

Recommended:
    Small environments only

Configuration:
--------------
Manage Jenkins
  ->
Security
  ->
Authorization

Select:
    Logged-in users can do anything

Result:
-------
Any authenticated LDAP user receives admin privileges.

WARNING:
--------
NOT recommended for enterprise production.

================================================================================
OPTION 2 : MATRIX-BASED SECURITY (RECOMMENDED)
================================================================================

Recommended:
    Enterprise production environments

Configuration:
--------------
Manage Jenkins
  ->
Security
  ->
Authorization

Select:
    Matrix-based security

================================================================================
RECOMMENDED MATRIX CONFIGURATION
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ADMIN USERS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User:
    jenkins-admins

Permissions:
    Overall/Administer
    Credentials/*
    Job/*
    View/*
    Run/*
    SCM/*
    Agent/*
    SystemRead/*

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
OPERATORS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User:
    jenkins-operators

Permissions:
    Overall/Read
    Job/Read
    Job/Build
    Job/Cancel
    View/Read

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
READ-ONLY USERS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User:
    jenkins-viewers

Permissions:
    Overall/Read
    Job/Read
    View/Read

================================================================================
RECOMMENDED LDAP GROUP STRATEGY
================================================================================

Create LDAP Groups:
-------------------

CN=jenkins-admins
CN=jenkins-operators
CN=jenkins-viewers

Assign users to groups in LDAP.

Map groups in Jenkins Matrix Authorization.

================================================================================
OPTION 3 : ROLE-BASED AUTHORIZATION STRATEGY
================================================================================

Recommended:
    Large enterprise environments

Requires Plugin:
    Role-based Authorization Strategy

Benefits:
---------
- Fine-grained permissions
- Easier management
- Folder-level permissions
- Project isolation

================================================================================
INFORMATION ACCESS RESTRICTION (SECTION 8.3)
================================================================================

PURPOSE:
--------
Restrict unauthorized information exposure in Jenkins.

================================================================================
RECOMMENDED CONTROLS
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1) DISABLE ANONYMOUS ACCESS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Security
  ->
Authorization

Remove:
    Anonymous users

Result:
    Unauthenticated users cannot view Jenkins.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
2) RESTRICT SCRIPT CONSOLE
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Grant:
    Script Console access ONLY to Jenkins admins.

Risk:
    Script Console provides full server access.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
3) RESTRICT CREDENTIAL VIEW ACCESS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Only Jenkins admins should have:
    Credentials/View
    Credentials/Create
    Credentials/Update

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
4) RESTRICT JOB CONFIGURATION
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Operators:
    Can build jobs

Admins:
    Can modify jobs

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
5) HIDE BUILD LOGS FROM NON-ADMINS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use:
    Matrix-based security

Restrict:
    Job/Read permissions

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
6) RESTRICT WORKSPACE ACCESS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Disable:
    Workspace browsing for regular users.

Reason:
    Sensitive files may exist in workspace.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
7) DISABLE CLI REMOTING (RECOMMENDED)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manage Jenkins
  ->
Security
  ->
Disable CLI over Remoting

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
8) ENABLE CSRF PROTECTION
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manage Jenkins
  ->
Security

Enable:
    Prevent Cross Site Request Forgery exploits

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
9) ENABLE AGENT → MASTER ACCESS CONTROL
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manage Jenkins
  ->
Security

Enable:
    Agent → Controller Access Control

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
10) RESTRICT BUILD TRIGGERS
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Only authorized users should:
    Trigger production patching

Use:
    Matrix authorization

================================================================================
LDAP TROUBLESHOOTING
================================================================================

SYMPTOM:
    Invalid Credentials

CAUSE:
    Wrong Manager DN or password

FIX:
    Verify bind account credentials

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SYMPTOM:
    User not found

CAUSE:
    Wrong search filter

FIX:
    Use:
        uid={0}
    OR
        sAMAccountName={0}

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SYMPTOM:
    Cannot connect to LDAP server

CAUSE:
    Firewall or DNS issue

FIX:
    Check:
        ping
        telnet
        firewall

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SYMPTOM:
    Groups not resolving

CAUSE:
    Wrong Group Search Base

FIX:
    Verify LDAP group OU path

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SYMPTOM:
    TLS/SSL certificate error

CAUSE:
    LDAP certificate not trusted

FIX:
    Import CA certificate into Java truststore

================================================================================
LDAP SECURITY BEST PRACTICES
================================================================================

[✓] Use LDAPS (636) instead of LDAP (389)

[✓] Use dedicated LDAP service account

[✓] Service account should be read-only

[✓] Rotate LDAP bind passwords regularly

[✓] Enable Matrix-based authorization

[✓] Disable anonymous Jenkins access

[✓] Restrict Script Console access

[✓] Use enterprise LDAP groups

[✓] Enable CSRF protection

[✓] Audit Jenkins admin access regularly

================================================================================
POST-CONFIGURATION VALIDATION
================================================================================

VALIDATION CHECKLIST
--------------------

[ ] LDAP Plugin installed

[ ] Jenkins restarted successfully

[ ] LDAP connection test successful

[ ] LDAP user login successful

[ ] Matrix authorization enabled

[ ] Anonymous access disabled

[ ] Admin groups mapped correctly

[ ] Operators restricted appropriately

[ ] HTTPS working

[ ] CSRF protection enabled

================================================================================
RESTART JENKINS AFTER LDAP CONFIGURATION
================================================================================

systemctl restart jenkins

Verify:
    systemctl status jenkins

================================================================================
FINAL LDAP VALIDATION
================================================================================

1. Open:
       https://jenkinspreprod.local

2. Login using LDAP user

3. Verify:
       Dashboard accessible

4. Verify:
       Correct permissions assigned

5. Verify:
       Unauthorized users blocked

SECTION 12.1: COMPREHENSIVE VALIDATION CHECKLIST

          Command: hostname
          Expected: jenkinspreprod.local

          Expected: System clock synchronized: yes

          Expected: https and ssh services allowed

          Expected: Enforcing

          Expected: httpd_can_network_connect --> on

----------------------------

          Command: systemctl status jenkins
          Expected: active (running)

          Command: ss -tlnp | grep 8080
          Expected: 127.0.0.1:8080 LISTEN

          Command: java -version
          Expected: openjdk version "21.0.5"

          Command: ls -ld /var/lib/jenkins
          Expected: drwxr-x--- jenkins jenkins

          Expected: No critical errors (warnings acceptable)

          Expected: active (running)

          Expected: 0.0.0.0:80 and 0.0.0.0:443 LISTEN

[ ] T9.7  netfilter-persistent active
          Command: ssh svc_ans@192.168.68.110 "systemctl status netfilter-persistent"
          Expected: active (exited)

          Expected: running

          Command: ssh svc_ans@192.168.121.150 "firewall-cmd --list-rich-rules"
          Expected: Rich rule for 192.168.121.182 present

================================================================================
PART 13: BACKUP & RECOVERY
================================================================================

This section provides comprehensive backup and recovery procedures to protect
the Jenkins Ansible automation platform.

BACKUP STRATEGY:
- Daily automated backups
- 30-day retention for daily backups
- 90-day retention for weekly backups
- Off-site backup storage recommended
- Regular restore testing

CRITICAL DATA TO PROTECT:
- Jenkins configuration and jobs
- Ansible playbooks and inventory
- SSL certificates and keys
- SSH keys
- Service account configurations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 13.1: CRITICAL FILES TO BACKUP
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Identify all critical files that must be backed up

CATEGORIZATION: By importance and change frequency


TIER 1 - CRITICAL (Backup Daily):
----------------------------------

Jenkins:
  /var/lib/jenkins/                                  # Entire Jenkins home
  /var/lib/jenkins/config.xml                        # Main configuration
  /var/lib/jenkins/jobs/                             # All job configurations
  /var/lib/jenkins/credentials.xml                   # Encrypted credentials
  /var/lib/jenkins/secrets/                          # Secret keys
  /var/lib/jenkins/users/                            # User accounts
  /var/lib/jenkins/plugins/                          # Installed plugins
  /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/known_hosts                  # SSH known hosts

Ansible:
  /home/svc_ans/ansible/                             # Ansible directory
  /home/svc_ans/ansible/hosts                        # Inventory
  /home/svc_ans/ansible/playbooks/                   # All playbooks
  /home/svc_ans/ansible/group_vars/                  # Group variables
  /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg                          # Ansible config
  /etc/ansible/ansible.cfg                           # System Ansible config
  /etc/ansible/hosts                                 # System inventory
  /etc/ansible/playbooks/                            # System playbooks

SSH Keys:
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa                          # Private key
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa.pub                      # Public key
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/config                          # SSH config
  /home/svc_ans/.ssh/known_hosts                     # Known hosts


TIER 2 - IMPORTANT (Backup Weekly):
------------------------------------

NGINX:
  /etc/nginx/conf.d/jenkins.conf                     # NGINX config
  /etc/nginx/conf.d/00-rate-limit.conf               # Rate limiting
  /etc/nginx/nginx.conf                              # Main NGINX config

SSL Certificates:
  /etc/ssl/certs/jenkins.crt                         # SSL certificate
  /etc/ssl/private/jenkins.key                       # SSL private key
  /etc/ssl/certs/dhparam.pem                         # DH parameters

Service Accounts:
  /etc/sudoers.d/svc_ans                             # Sudo config
  /etc/passwd                                         # User accounts
  /etc/group                                          # Group memberships
  /etc/shadow                                         # Password hashes (encrypted backup)

Firewall:
  /etc/firewalld/zones/                              # Firewalld zones (Oracle Linux)
  /etc/iptables/rules.v4                             # iptables rules (Ubuntu)


TIER 3 - CONFIGURATION (Backup Monthly):
-----------------------------------------

System Configuration:
  /etc/hosts                                          # Host resolution
  /etc/hostname                                       # Hostname
  /etc/chrony.conf                                    # Time sync config
  /etc/systemd/system/jenkins.service.d/              # Jenkins systemd overrides
  /etc/fail2ban/jail.d/                              # Fail2ban configuration


Python Virtual Environment:
  /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/requirements.txt        # Python packages list
  NOTE: Full venv is large, backup requirements.txt only


Logs (Optional - For Audit):
  /var/log/jenkins/                                  # Jenkins logs (last 30 days)
  /var/log/nginx/                                    # NGINX logs (last 30 days)
  /home/svc_ans/logs/                                # Ansible logs (last 30 days)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 13.2: BACKUP SCRIPT
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Automated backup script for all critical files

EXECUTION: Run as root on control node


Create Backup Script:
---------------------

cat > /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh << 'BACKUPSCRIPT'
#!/bin/bash
################################################################################
# JENKINS ANSIBLE PLATFORM BACKUP SCRIPT
# Version: 2.0
# Description: Comprehensive backup of Jenkins, Ansible, and configurations
# Author: Infrastructure Team
# Date: January 2026
################################################################################

set -euo pipefail

# ==============================================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ==============================================================================

# Backup destination
BACKUP_BASE_DIR="/backup"
OFFSITE_BACKUP_DIR="/mnt/offsite-backup"  # Mount point for offsite storage

# Retention periods (days)
DAILY_RETENTION=30
WEEKLY_RETENTION=90
MONTHLY_RETENTION=365

# Timestamp
TIMESTAMP=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)
DATE_STAMP=$(date +%Y%m%d)
DAY_OF_WEEK=$(date +%u)  # 1=Monday, 7=Sunday
DAY_OF_MONTH=$(date +%d)

# Determine backup type
if [ "$DAY_OF_MONTH" == "01" ]; then
    BACKUP_TYPE="monthly"
    RETENTION_DAYS=$MONTHLY_RETENTION
elif [ "$DAY_OF_WEEK" == "7" ]; then
    BACKUP_TYPE="weekly"
    RETENTION_DAYS=$WEEKLY_RETENTION
else
    BACKUP_TYPE="daily"
    RETENTION_DAYS=$DAILY_RETENTION
fi

# Backup directory
BACKUP_DIR="${BACKUP_BASE_DIR}/jenkins-ansible-${BACKUP_TYPE}-${TIMESTAMP}"

# Logging
LOG_FILE="/var/log/backup-jenkins-ansible.log"

# ==============================================================================
# FUNCTIONS
# ==============================================================================

log_info() {
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [INFO] $*" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

log_error() {
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [ERROR] $*" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE" >&2
}

log_warning() {
    echo "[$(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [WARNING] $*" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

check_prerequisites() {
    log_info "Checking prerequisites..."
    
    # Check if running as root
    if [ "$EUID" -ne 0 ]; then
        log_error "This script must be run as root"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    # Check backup directory exists
    if [ ! -d "$BACKUP_BASE_DIR" ]; then
        log_info "Creating backup directory: $BACKUP_BASE_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$BACKUP_BASE_DIR"
    fi
    
    # Check disk space (require at least 10GB free)
    AVAILABLE_SPACE=$(df -BG "$BACKUP_BASE_DIR" | awk 'NR==2 {print $4}' | sed 's/G//')
    if [ "$AVAILABLE_SPACE" -lt 10 ]; then
        log_warning "Low disk space: ${AVAILABLE_SPACE}GB available"
    fi
    
    log_info "Prerequisites check passed"
}

create_backup_directory() {
    log_info "Creating backup directory: $BACKUP_DIR"
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR"
    
    if [ ! -d "$BACKUP_DIR" ]; then
        log_error "Failed to create backup directory"
        exit 1
    fi
}

backup_jenkins() {
    log_info "Backing up Jenkins home directory..."
    
    # Stop Jenkins for consistent backup (optional - comment out for hot backup)
    # systemctl stop jenkins
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-home.tar.gz" \
        /var/lib/jenkins/ \
        --exclude=/var/lib/jenkins/workspace \
        --exclude=/var/lib/jenkins/war \
        --exclude=/var/lib/jenkins/cache \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some Jenkins files inaccessible (normal)"
    
    # Restart Jenkins if stopped
    # systemctl start jenkins
    
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-home.tar.gz" ]; then
        log_info "Jenkins backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-home.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    else
        log_error "Jenkins backup failed"
        return 1
    fi
}

backup_nginx() {
    log_info "Backing up NGINX configuration..."
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/nginx-config.tar.gz" \
        /etc/nginx/conf.d/ \
        /etc/nginx/nginx.conf \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some NGINX files inaccessible"
    
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/nginx-config.tar.gz" ]; then
        log_info "NGINX backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/nginx-config.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    else
        log_error "NGINX backup failed"
        return 1
    fi
}

backup_ssl() {
    log_info "Backing up SSL certificates..."
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz" \
        /etc/ssl/certs/jenkins.crt \
        /etc/ssl/private/jenkins.key \
        /etc/ssl/certs/dhparam.pem \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some SSL files inaccessible"
    
    # Encrypt SSL backup (contains private key)
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz" ]; then
        # Set restrictive permissions
        chmod 600 "$BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz"
        log_info "SSL backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    else
        log_error "SSL backup failed"
        return 1
    fi
}

backup_ansible() {
    log_info "Backing up Ansible configuration..."
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-config.tar.gz" \
        /home/svc_ans/ansible/ \
        /home/svc_ans/ansible.cfg \
        /etc/ansible/ \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some Ansible files inaccessible"
    
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-config.tar.gz" ]; then
        log_info "Ansible config backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/ansible-config.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    else
        log_error "Ansible config backup failed"
        return 1
    fi
}

backup_ssh_keys() {
    log_info "Backing up SSH keys..."
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz" \
        /home/svc_ans/.ssh/ \
        /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh/ \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some SSH files inaccessible"
    
    # Encrypt SSH backup (contains private keys)
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz" ]; then
        chmod 600 "$BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz"
        log_info "SSH keys backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    else
        log_error "SSH keys backup failed"
        return 1
    fi
}

backup_venv_requirements() {
    log_info "Backing up Python virtual environment requirements..."
    
    if [ -f "/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/requirements.txt" ]; then
        cp /home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/requirements.txt \
           "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-venv-requirements.txt" 2>/dev/null
        log_info "Venv requirements backed up"
    else
        log_warning "Venv requirements.txt not found"
    fi
}

backup_system_config() {
    log_info "Backing up system configuration..."
    
    tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/system-config.tar.gz" \
        /etc/sudoers.d/svc_ans \
        /etc/hosts \
        /etc/hostname \
        /etc/chrony.conf \
        /etc/systemd/system/jenkins.service.d/ \
        /etc/fail2ban/jail.d/ \
        /etc/firewalld/zones/ \
        2>/dev/null || log_warning "Some system config files inaccessible"
    
    if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/system-config.tar.gz" ]; then
        log_info "System config backup completed: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR/system-config.tar.gz | cut -f1)"
    fi
}

backup_firewall_rules() {
    log_info "Backing up firewall rules..."
    
    # Firewalld rules
    firewall-cmd --list-all > "$BACKUP_DIR/firewalld-rules.txt" 2>/dev/null || true
    
    # iptables rules (if exists)
    if [ -f "/etc/iptables/rules.v4" ]; then
        cp /etc/iptables/rules.v4 "$BACKUP_DIR/iptables-rules.v4" 2>/dev/null || true
    fi
    
    log_info "Firewall rules backed up"
}

backup_logs() {
    log_info "Backing up recent logs (last 7 days)..."
    
    # Jenkins logs
    if [ -d "/var/log/jenkins" ]; then
        find /var/log/jenkins -type f -mtime -7 -print0 | \
            tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-logs-7days.tar.gz" --null -T - 2>/dev/null || true
    fi
    
    # NGINX logs
    find /var/log/nginx -type f -name "jenkins*.log*" -mtime -7 -print0 | \
        tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/nginx-logs-7days.tar.gz" --null -T - 2>/dev/null || true
    
    # Ansible logs
    if [ -d "/home/svc_ans/logs" ]; then
        find /home/svc_ans/logs -type f -mtime -7 -print0 | \
            tar czf "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-logs-7days.tar.gz" --null -T - 2>/dev/null || true
    fi
    
    log_info "Logs backup completed"
}

create_manifest() {
    log_info "Creating backup manifest..."
    
    cat > "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt" << EOF
================================================================================
JENKINS ANSIBLE PLATFORM BACKUP MANIFEST
================================================================================

Backup Type    : ${BACKUP_TYPE}
Backup Date    : $(date +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
Hostname       : $(hostname)
Backup Location: ${BACKUP_DIR}
Created By     : $(whoami)

================================================================================
BACKUP CONTENTS
================================================================================

EOF

    # List all files with sizes
    ls -lh "$BACKUP_DIR" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    
    echo "" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "================================================================================" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "TOTAL BACKUP SIZE" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "================================================================================" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    du -sh "$BACKUP_DIR" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    
    echo "" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "================================================================================" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "SYSTEM INFORMATION" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "================================================================================" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "Kernel: $(uname -r)" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "OS: $(cat /etc/os-release | grep PRETTY_NAME | cut -d'"' -f2)" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "Jenkins Version: $(systemctl show jenkins -p MainPID --value | xargs -I {} ps -p {} -o args= | grep -oP 'jenkins-\K[0-9.]+')" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "Ansible 2.9 Version: $(/usr/bin/ansible --version | head -1)" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    echo "Ansible 6.7 Version: $(/home/svc_ans/ansible-venv/bin/ansible --version | head -1)" >> "$BACKUP_DIR/MANIFEST.txt"
    
    log_info "Manifest created"
}

create_restore_script() {
    log_info "Creating restore script..."
    
    cat > "$BACKUP_DIR/RESTORE.sh" << 'RESTORESCRIPT'
#!/bin/bash
################################################################################
# RESTORE SCRIPT FOR JENKINS ANSIBLE PLATFORM
# WARNING: This will overwrite existing configurations
################################################################################

set -euo pipefail

BACKUP_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"

echo "==========================================="
echo "JENKINS ANSIBLE PLATFORM RESTORE"
echo "==========================================="
echo "Backup Directory: $BACKUP_DIR"
echo "This will restore all configurations"
echo "WARNING: This will overwrite current config"
echo "==========================================="
read -p "Are you sure you want to proceed? (yes/no): " CONFIRM

if [ "$CONFIRM" != "yes" ]; then
    echo "Restore cancelled"
    exit 0
fi

echo "Starting restore..."

# Restore Jenkins
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-home.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Stopping Jenkins..."
    systemctl stop jenkins
    
    echo "Restoring Jenkins home..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/jenkins-home.tar.gz" -C /
    chown -R jenkins:jenkins /var/lib/jenkins
    
    echo "Starting Jenkins..."
    systemctl start jenkins
fi

# Restore NGINX
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/nginx-config.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Restoring NGINX configuration..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/nginx-config.tar.gz" -C /
    nginx -t && systemctl restart nginx
fi

# Restore SSL
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Restoring SSL certificates..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/ssl-certificates.tar.gz" -C /
    chmod 600 /etc/ssl/private/jenkins.key
    chmod 644 /etc/ssl/certs/jenkins.crt
fi

# Restore Ansible
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-config.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Restoring Ansible configuration..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/ansible-config.tar.gz" -C /
    chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/ansible
fi

# Restore SSH keys
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Restoring SSH keys..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/ssh-keys.tar.gz" -C /
    chown -R svc_ans:svc_ans /home/svc_ans/.ssh
    chmod 700 /home/svc_ans/.ssh
    chmod 600 /home/svc_ans/.ssh/id_rsa
    chown -R jenkins:jenkins /var/lib/jenkins/.ssh
fi

# Restore system config
if [ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/system-config.tar.gz" ]; then
    echo "Restoring system configuration..."
    tar xzf "$BACKUP_DIR/system-config.tar.gz" -C /
fi

echo "==========================================="
echo "RESTORE COMPLETED"
echo "==========================================="
echo "Please verify all services are running:"
echo "  systemctl status jenkins"
echo "  systemctl status nginx"
echo "  systemctl status firewalld"
echo "==========================================="
RESTORESCRIPT

    chmod 755 "$BACKUP_DIR/RESTORE.sh"
    log_info "Restore script created"
}

set_permissions() {
    log_info "Setting backup permissions..."
    
    # Secure backup directory
    chmod 700 "$BACKUP_DIR"
    
    # Secure sensitive files
    find "$BACKUP_DIR" -name "*ssh-keys*" -exec chmod 600 {} \;
    find "$BACKUP_DIR" -name "*ssl-certificates*" -exec chmod 600 {} \;
    
    log_info "Permissions set"
}

copy_to_offsite() {
    if [ -d "$OFFSITE_BACKUP_DIR" ] && mountpoint -q "$OFFSITE_BACKUP_DIR"; then
        log_info "Copying backup to offsite location..."
        
        rsync -az --delete-after "$BACKUP_DIR/" "${OFFSITE_BACKUP_DIR}/jenkins-ansible-${BACKUP_TYPE}-${DATE_STAMP}/"
        
        if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
            log_info "Offsite backup completed"
        else
            log_warning "Offsite backup failed"
        fi
    else
        log_warning "Offsite backup directory not available, skipping"
    fi
}

cleanup_old_backups() {
    log_info "Cleaning up old backups (retention: ${RETENTION_DAYS} days)..."
    
    # Remove old backups of same type
    find "$BACKUP_BASE_DIR" -type d -name "jenkins-ansible-${BACKUP_TYPE}-*" -mtime +${RETENTION_DAYS} -exec rm -rf {} \; 2>/dev/null || true
    
    # Count remaining backups
    BACKUP_COUNT=$(find "$BACKUP_BASE_DIR" -type d -name "jenkins-ansible-*" | wc -l)
    log_info "Total backups retained: $BACKUP_COUNT"
}

verify_backup() {
    log_info "Verifying backup integrity..."
    
    # Check all critical files exist
    CRITICAL_FILES=(
        "jenkins-home.tar.gz"
        "nginx-config.tar.gz"
        "ssl-certificates.tar.gz"
        "ansible-config.tar.gz"
        "ssh-keys.tar.gz"
        "MANIFEST.txt"
        "RESTORE.sh"
    )
    
    MISSING=0
    for file in "${CRITICAL_FILES[@]}"; do
        if [ ! -f "$BACKUP_DIR/$file" ]; then
            log_error "Missing critical file: $file"
            MISSING=$((MISSING + 1))
        fi
    done
    
    if [ $MISSING -eq 0 ]; then
        log_info "Backup verification passed (all critical files present)"
        return 0
    else
        log_error "Backup verification failed (${MISSING} files missing)"
        return 1
    fi
}

send_notification() {
    local status=$1
    local message=$2
    
    # Email notification (configure mail server first)
    # echo "$message" | mail -s "Backup Status: $status" admin@example.com
    
    # Log notification
    if [ "$status" == "SUCCESS" ]; then
        log_info "BACKUP COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY"
    else
        log_error "BACKUP FAILED: $message"
    fi
}

# ==============================================================================
# MAIN EXECUTION
# ==============================================================================

main() {
    log_info "==========================================="
    log_info "JENKINS ANSIBLE PLATFORM BACKUP STARTED"
    log_info "==========================================="
    log_info "Backup Type: ${BACKUP_TYPE}"
    log_info "Timestamp: ${TIMESTAMP}"
    log_info "Retention: ${RETENTION_DAYS} days"
    
    # Check prerequisites
    check_prerequisites
    
    # Create backup directory
    create_backup_directory
    
    # Perform backups
    backup_jenkins
    backup_nginx
    backup_ssl
    backup_ansible
    backup_ssh_keys
    backup_venv_requirements
    backup_system_config
    backup_firewall_rules
    backup_logs
    
    # Create manifest and restore script
    create_manifest
    create_restore_script
    
    # Set permissions
    set_permissions
    
    # Verify backup
    if verify_backup; then
        # Copy to offsite if available
        copy_to_offsite
        
        # Cleanup old backups
        cleanup_old_backups
        
        # Send success notification
        send_notification "SUCCESS" "Backup completed successfully"
        
        log_info "==========================================="
        log_info "BACKUP COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY"
        log_info "==========================================="
        log_info "Backup Location: $BACKUP_DIR"
        log_info "Backup Size: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR | cut -f1)"
        log_info "==========================================="
        
        exit 0
    else
        send_notification "FAILED" "Backup verification failed"
        log_error "BACKUP FAILED"
        exit 1
    fi
}

# Execute main function
main
BACKUPSCRIPT


# Make backup script executable
chmod 755 /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh

# Verify script created
ls -la /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh


BACKUP SCRIPT FEATURES:
-----------------------

1. Backup Type Detection:
   - Daily backups (30-day retention)
   - Weekly backups (90-day retention)
   - Monthly backups (365-day retention)

2. Comprehensive Coverage:
   - Jenkins home directory
   - NGINX configuration
   - SSL certificates (encrypted)
   - Ansible configurations
   - SSH keys (encrypted)
   - System configuration
   - Recent logs

3. Safety Features:
   - Prerequisite checks
   - Disk space verification
   - Backup verification
   - Secure permissions
   - Error handling

4. Recovery Support:
   - Automatic restore script generation
   - Backup manifest
   - System information snapshot

5. Retention Management:
   - Automatic cleanup of old backups
   - Configurable retention periods

6. Offsite Backup:
   - Rsync to offsite location
   - Optional encrypted transfer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SECTION 13.3: AUTOMATED BACKUP (CRON)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PURPOSE: Schedule automated backups

EXECUTION: Configure cron on control node as root


Method 1: System-wide crontab (/etc/crontab):
----------------------------------------------

# Edit system crontab
vi /etc/crontab

# Add backup job (runs daily at 2 AM)
0 2 * * * root /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh >> /var/log/backup-jenkins-ansible.log 2>&1


Method 2: Root crontab (crontab -e):
-------------------------------------

# Edit root crontab
crontab -e

# Add backup job
0 2 * * * /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh >> /var/log/backup-jenkins-ansible.log 2>&1


Method 3: Systemd Timer (Modern Alternative):
----------------------------------------------

# Create systemd service
cat > /etc/systemd/system/jenkins-backup.service << 'EOF'
[Unit]
Description=Jenkins Ansible Platform Backup
After=network.target

[Service]
Type=oneshot
ExecStart=/usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh
User=root
StandardOutput=journal
StandardError=journal
EOF


# Create systemd timer
cat > /etc/systemd/system/jenkins-backup.timer << 'EOF'
[Unit]
Description=Daily Jenkins Ansible Platform Backup
Requires=jenkins-backup.service

[Timer]
OnCalendar=daily
OnCalendar=*-*-* 02:00:00
Persistent=true

[Install]
WantedBy=timers.target
EOF


# Enable and start timer
systemctl daemon-reload
systemctl enable jenkins-backup.timer
systemctl start jenkins-backup.timer

# Verify timer is active
systemctl list-timers --all | grep jenkins-backup


SCHEDULE RECOMMENDATIONS:
-------------------------

Development Environment:
- Daily backups at 2 AM
- 7-day retention

Production Environment:
- Daily backups at 2 AM (30-day retention)
- Weekly backups on Sunday (90-day retention)
- Monthly backups on 1st day (365-day retention)
- Offsite sync after each backup


CRON SCHEDULE EXAMPLES:
-----------------------

Daily at 2 AM:
0 2 * * * /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh

Every 6 hours:
0 */6 * * * /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh

Weekly on Sunday at 3 AM:
0 3 * * 0 /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh

Monthly on 1st at 4 AM:
0 4 1 * * /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh

Twice daily (2 AM and 2 PM):
0 2,14 * * * /usr/local/bin/backup-jenkins-ansible.sh
